### Rape of a courtier

# Rape of a courtier (not close relative)
narrative_event = {	
	id = DWT.020
	desc = EVTDESCDWT.020
	picture = GFX_evt_DWTr005
	
	is_triggered_only = yes		# triggered from a rape decision
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTDWT.020
		hidden_tooltip = { 
			from = {
				opinion = {	# she will hate you
					modifier = opinion_raped_me
					who = ROOT
				}
				opinion = {	# she will hate you more for a brief time
					modifier = raper_ruler
					who = ROOT
				}
			}
			piety = -20		# you loose some piety
			add_character_modifier = { name = dw_good_sex duration = 30 }
		}
		narrative_event = { id = DWT.200 }
	}
}

# Rape of a courtier (not close relative, but brave), who fights back 1/3
narrative_event = {	
	id = DWT.024
	desc = EVTDESCDWT.024
	picture = GFX_evt_DWTr005
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTDWT.024
		hidden_tooltip = { 
			from = {	
				add_trait = wounded	# the victim will be wounded
				opinion = {		# and she will hate you
					modifier = opinion_raped_me
					who = ROOT
				}
				opinion = {		# she will hate you more for a brief time
					modifier = raper_ruler
					who = ROOT
				}
			}
			piety = -25			# you loose some piety
			add_character_modifier = { name = dw_good_sex duration = 30 }
			random = {			# there is 25% chance you'll be wounded
				chance = 25
				add_trait = wounded
			}
			random = {			# there is 5% chance something terrible happens with you, see below
				chance = 5
				from = { 
					narrative_event = { id = DWT.025 }
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# Rape of a courtier (not close relative, but brave), who fights back 1/4 (death path)

}

# Rape of a courtier (but it's not rape if she wants it)
narrative_event = {	
	id = DWT.027
	desc = EVTDESCDWT.027
	picture = GFX_evt_DWTr012
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTDWT.027
		hidden_tooltip = { 
			FROM = {
				remove_trait = shy
				remove_trait = chaste
				remove_trait = celibate
				remove_trait = depressed
				add_trait = lustful
				add_trait = ambitious
				add_lover = ROOT
				remove_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_took_virginity_by_force }
				add_character_modifier = { name = dw_good_sex duration = 30 }
			}
		}
		add_character_modifier = { name = dw_good_sex duration = 30 }
		narrative_event = { id = DWT.200 }
	}
}

# Rape of a close relative (but it's not rape if she wants it)

		hidden_tooltip = {

				remove_trait = celibate
				remove_trait = depressed
				random = {
					chance = 50
					add_trait = lustful
				}
				random = {
					chance = 25
					add_trait = ambitious
				}	
				add_lover = ROOT
				remove_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_took_virginity_by_force }
				add_character_modifier = { name = dw_good_sex duration = 30 }
			}
			add_character_modifier = { name = dw_good_sex duration = 30 }
		}
		narrative_event = { id = DWT.200 }
	}
}

######### Torturing prisoners for the truly evil #########

# .500 Procreo command dog owner bounce (dog owner)
character_event = {
	id = DWT.500
	
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		
		FROM = { narrative_event = { id = DWT.501 }} # target decides their action
	}
}
# .501 Guard Dog mates on command with target (target)
narrative_event = {
	id = DWT.501
	desc = "DWT501"
	picture = DWE_Prisoner
	title = dw_guard_dog_procreo
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = "DWT501B" # Struggle
		tooltip_info = martial
		FROM = { character_event = { id = DWT.510 }} # Bounce to the dog owner
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					trait = beast_lover
					has_character_modifier = werewolf_bitch
					}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				OR = {
				trait = lustful
				trait = hedonist
				}
			}
			
		}
	}	
	option = {
				trigger = {
			OR = {			
				trait = lustful
				trait = hedonist
				trait = beast_lover
				has_character_modifier = werewolf_bitch
			}
		}

		name = "DWT501C" # Submit willingly
		FROM = { narrative_event = { id = DWT.540 }} # Dog owner's perspective
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.20
				NOR = {
					trait = beast_lover
					has_character_modifier = werewolf_bitch
					}
					
			
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		trigger = {
			has_character_modifier = alpha_bitch
		}
		name = "DWT501D" # Intimidate the beast
		custom_tooltip = { text = dw_alpha_bitch_beats_dog }
		FROM = {
			opinion = {
				modifier = opinion_intimidated
				who = ROOT
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
	}
}

# .511 Guard dog rapes prisoner  (target)
narrative_event = {
	id = DWT.511
	desc = "DWT511"
	picture = DWBuilding_GuardDog_Precreo
	title = dw_guard_dog_procreo
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = "DWT511A"
		hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = DWCore.9100 }} #Remove Virgin check
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { trait = victim }
			}
			add_trait = victim
		}
		opinion = {
			modifier = dw_opinion_bad_dog_raper_owner 
			who = FROM
		}
	}
}

				change_learning = 100
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				ROOT = {
					NOT = {
						trait = yiminhyee
					}
				}
			}
		random = {
				chance = 30
				if = {
					limit = {
						FROMFROMFROMFROM = {
								is_female = yes
								is_pregnant = no
								fertility = 0.1
								NOT = {
									age = 40
								}
							}
						is_female = no
					}
					FROMFROMFROMFROM = { 
						impregnate_cuckoo = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# Lilith women generals can gangbang their troops
narrative_event = {
	id = DWT.900
	is_triggered_only = yes
	desc = DWT900desc
	picture = GFX_event_nada3
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_war

	option = {
		name = DWT900option
		#add_character_modifier = {
		#	name = troops_gangbanged_general
		#	duration = 30
		#}
		add_character_modifier = { name = dwt_morale_booster duration = 30 }
		ROOT = { 
			if = {
				limit = {
					trait = virgin
				}
				remove_trait = virgin 
			}
		}        
        hidden_tooltip = {
			# Another general in the gangbang, if available
			any_realm_character = {
				limit = {
					is_female = no
					is_adult = yes
					in_command = yes
					ai = yes
					NOT = {
						trait = chaste
						trait = celibate
						trait = incapable
						spouse = { character = ROOT }
						is_lover = ROOT
					}
				}
				narrative_event = { id = DWT.902 }
			}        
			# If she's still not pregnant, one of her (non-character) soldiers
			# has a good chance to do it.
			if = {
				limit = {
				    is_pregnant = no
					OR = {
						fertility = 0.1
						trait = celibate #this way we ignore celibacy's penalty, because you're sure as shit not being celibate here
					}
				    NOT = { practical_age = 45 }
				}
				random = {
					chance = 50
					impregnate = 0
				}
			}
			
			if = {
				limit = { trait = weak }
				random = {
					chance = 10
					add_trait = ill
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { trait = strong } }
				random = {
					chance = 5
					add_trait = ill
				}
			}
			hidden_tooltip = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							trait = celibate
							}
						remove_trait = celibate
				
					}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { is_married = yes }
				add_character_modifier = { name = adulteress duration = 180 }
			}
        }
	}
}

# Tumble impregnation chance event
narrative_event = {
	id = DWT.903
	
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		
		# AI affair pregnancy limiter
		if = {
			limit = {
				ai = yes
				FROM = { ai = yes }
				has_character_modifier = lustful_affair_timer
			}
			break = yes
		}
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = lustful_affair_timer
			duration = 2190
			hidden = yes
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_female = no
					practical_age = 45
					is_pregnant = yes
					FROM = { is_female = yes }
					NOT = { fertility = 0.2 }
					NOT = { FROM = { fertility = 0.2 } }
				}
			}
			break  = yes
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_pregnant = yes
					FROM = { is_pregnant = yes }
				}
			}
			break = yes
		}
	
		# Chance of impregnation
		if = {
			limit = {
				fertility = 0.6
				OR = {
					ai = no
					NOT = { num_of_children = 4 }
				}
				FROM = {
					fertility = 0.6
					OR = {
						ai = no
						NOT = { num_of_children = 4 }
					}
				}
			}
			random = {
				chance = 50
				if = {
					limit = {
						is_married = no
						is_consort = no
					}
					impregnate = FROM
					break = yes
				}
				impregnate_cuckoo = FROM
			}
			break = yes
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				fertility = 0.5
				OR = {
					ai = no
					NOT = { num_of_children = 6 }
				}
				FROM = {
					fertility = 0.5
					OR = {
						ai = no
						NOT = { num_of_children = 6 }
					}
				}
			}
			random = {
				chance = 33
				if = {
					limit = {
						is_married = no
						is_consort = no
					}
					impregnate = FROM
					break = yes
				}
				impregnate_cuckoo = FROM
			}
			break = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				fertility = 0.34
				FROM = { fertility = 0.34 }
			}
			random = {
				chance = 15
				if = {
					limit = {
						is_married = no
						is_consort = no
					}
					impregnate = FROM
					break = yes
				}
				impregnate_cuckoo = FROM
			}
			break = yes
		}
		
		random = {
			chance = 5
			if = {
				limit = {
					fertility = 0.1
					is_married = no
					is_consort = no
				}
				impregnate = FROM
				break = yes
			}
			impregnate_cuckoo = FROM
		}
	}
}

			in_command = yes
			is_adult = yes
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					FROM = {
						ai = yes #If the ai somehow triggered this, we simply kill the event
					}
				}
			}
			break = yes
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					is_female = yes
				}
			}
			FROM = {
				narrative_event = { id = DWT.921} #liege is a female
			}
			break = yes
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					is_female = no
				}
			}
			FROM = {
				#narrative_event = { id = DWT.925} #liege is a male - commented out for now
			}
			break = yes
		}
	}
}

# 1. Female liege ambushed while on patrol.
narrative_event = {	
	id = DWT.921
	desc = DWT921desc
	picture = TroopFemaleLiegeAmbush1
	is_triggered_only = yes		# triggered from DWT.920
	
	immediate = {
			

			if = {
                limit = {
                    any_mercenary_band = { 
                        holder_scope = {
                            has_character_flag = is_mercenary_leader
                            is_adult = yes
                            ai = yes
                            is_female = no
                        }
                    }
                }
                any_mercenary_band = {
                    holder_scope = {
                        limit = { #same base requirements
                            has_character_flag = is_mercenary_leader
                            is_adult = yes
                            ai = yes
                            is_female = no
                        }
					save_event_target_as = my_duel_target
                    set_character_flag = fought_duel_against@ROOT
                             
                    #REQUIRED event targets for setting up duel evaluation!
                    save_event_target_as = combatant_2 #the target of the duel...
                    ROOT = { save_event_target_as = combatant_1 } #the person issuing the duel...
					}
				}
			}
			else = { # No one available, spawn someone
                        spawn_great_commander_effect = yes
                        event_target:invited_character = {
                            upgrade_education_effect = yes
                            add_one_duel_experience_modifier = yes
                            save_event_target_as = my_duel_target
                            set_character_flag = fought_duel_against@ROOT
                            
                            #REQUIRED event targets for setting up duel evaluation!
                            save_event_target_as = combatant_2 #the target of the duel...
                            ROOT = { save_event_target_as = combatant_1 } #the person issuing the duel...
							banish = yes
                        }
                    }
	}
	option = { # submit
		name = DWT921option
		hidden_tooltip = { ROOT = { narrative_event = { id = DWT.922 } } }
		} 
	option = { # fight
		name = DWT921optiona
		hidden_tooltip = { ROOT = {narrative_event = { id = DWT.970 } } }
		}


}

# .940 Liege has an bathing encounter
narrative_event = {
	id = DWT.940
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hide_window = yes
	
	trigger = {
		NOT = { trait = futa }
		FROM = {
			ai = no
			prisoner = no
			in_command = yes
			is_adult = yes
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					FROM = {
						ai = yes #If the ai somehow triggered this, we simply kill the event
					}
				}
			}
			break = yes
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					is_female = yes
				}
			}
			FROM = {
				narrative_event = { id = DWT.941} #liege is a female
			}
			break = yes
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					is_female = no
				}
			}
			FROM = {
				narrative_event = { id = DWTRandom.945} #liege is a male
			}
			break = yes
		}
	}
}

	id = DWT.942
	desc = DWT942desc
	picture = DTW_FM_Bath2
	
	hide_from = yes			# it's a ping back, actually
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = DWT942option
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		hidden_tooltip = { FROM = { narrative_event = { id = DWT.943 } } }
	}
	option = {
		name = DWT942optiona
		random_list = {
				15 = {
					modifier = {
						factor = 2
						trait = wounded					
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 3
						trait = severely_injured					
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 4
						OR = {
						trait = one_legged					
						trait = mangled
						}
					}							
					death = {death_reason = death_murder }							
				}
				40 = {
					modifier = {
						factor = 2
						trait = weak					
					}							
					add_trait = severely_injured
					narrative_event = { id = DWT.949 }
				}
				20 = {
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.25
						trait = strong					
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.25
						trait = genius					
					}
					add_trait = wounded
					narrative_event = { id = DWT.949 }
				}
				25 = {
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.5
						trait = strong					
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.5
						trait = genius					
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.25
						trait = quick					
					}
					narrative_event = { id = DWT.949 }		
				}
			
		}

	
	}
}

	desc = DWT949desc
	picture = DTW_FM_Bath2
	
	is_triggered_only = yes	
	
	option = { # you make your escape
		name = DWT949optiona
		trigger = {
		OR = {
				AND = {
				combat_rating = 100
				NOR = {
				trait = mangled
				trait = one_legged							
					}
				}
				AND = {
				combat_rating = 75
				NOT = {
				trait = severely_injured
					}
				}
				AND = {
				combat_rating = 50
				NOT = {
				trait = wounded
					}
				}
				AND = {
				combat_rating = 25
				}
		
			}
		
		}

	}
	option = {
		name = DWT949optionb
		trigger = {
		NOR = {
				AND = {
				combat_rating = 100
				NOR = {
				trait = mangled
				trait = one_legged							
					}
				}
				AND = {
				combat_rating = 75
				NOT = {
				trait = severely_injured
					}
				}
				AND = {
				combat_rating = 50
				NOT = {
				trait = wounded
					}
				}
				AND = {
				combat_rating = 25
				}
		
			}
		
		}

		hidden_tooltip = { FROM = { narrative_event = { id = DWT.943 } } }
	}
	
	
}


#
### Sparring encounter

# .950 Liege is sparring with Lieutenant.
narrative_event = {
	id = DWT.950
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hide_window = yes
	
	trigger = {
		NOT = { trait = futa }
		FROM = {
			ai = no
			prisoner = no
			in_command = yes
			is_adult = yes
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					FROM = {
						ai = yes #If the ai somehow triggered this, we simply kill the event
					}
				}
			}
			break = yes
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					is_female = yes
				}
			}
			random_courtier_or_vassal = {
				limit = {
					has_minor_title = commander
					NOT = {is_female = yes }
				}
				save_event_target_as = dwt_sparring
			}
			FROM = {
				narrative_event = { id = DWT.951} #liege is a female
			}
			break = yes
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					is_female = no
				}
			}
			FROM = {
				narrative_event = { id = DWTRandom.955} #liege is a male
			}
			break = yes
		}
			random_courtier_or_vassal = {
				limit = {
					has_minor_title = commander
					NOT = {is_female = yes }
				}
				save_event_target_as = dwt_sparring


			}

	}
}

# 2. Female liege ambushed while on patrol - Tries to fight
narrative_event = {	
	id = DWT.970
	desc = DWT970desc
	picture = TroopFemaleLiegeAmbushFight
	
	hide_from = yes			# it's a ping back, actually
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	portrait = event_target:my_duel_target

	immediate = {

			event_target:my_duel_target = {
				if = {
                        limit = {
                            ROOT = { combat_rating_diff = { who = PREV value = 75 } } # if ROOT is 75 better
                        }
						random_list = {
						80 = {ROOT = { set_character_flag = won_ambush } }
						20 = {ROOT = { set_character_flag = lost_ambush } }
						# You're outnumbered so the other guy gets some help, even still
						}
					}
				else_if = {
                        limit = {
                            ROOT = { combat_rating_diff = { who = PREV value = 50 } } # if ROOT is 50 better
                        }
						random_list = {
						70 = {ROOT = { set_character_flag = won_ambush } }
						30 = {ROOT = { set_character_flag = lost_ambush } }
			
						}
					}
				else_if = {
                        limit = {
                            ROOT = { combat_rating_diff = { who = PREV value = 25 } } # if ROOT is 25 better
                        }
						random_list = {
						50 = {ROOT = { set_character_flag = won_ambush } }
						30 = {ROOT = { set_character_flag = lost_ambush } }
						20 = {ROOT = { set_character_flag = lost_ambush_bad } }
						}
					}
				else_if = {
                        limit = {
                            ROOT = { combat_rating_diff = { who = PREV value = 0 } } # if ROOT is 0 better
                        }
						random_list = {
						30 = {ROOT = { set_character_flag = won_ambush } }
						30 = {ROOT = { set_character_flag = lost_ambush } }
						40 = {ROOT = { set_character_flag = lost_ambush_bad } }			
						}
					}
				else_if = {
                        limit = {
                            ROOT = { combat_rating_diff = { who = PREV value = -25 } } # if ROOT is -25 worse						
                        }
						random_list = {
						10 = {ROOT = { set_character_flag = won_ambush } }
						30 = {ROOT = { set_character_flag = lost_ambush } }	
						60 = {ROOT = { set_character_flag = lost_ambush_bad } }						
						}
					}				
				else = { 
						random_list = { # if you're worse than 25, you automatically lose, just a question of how bad
						20 = {ROOT = { set_character_flag = lost_ambush } }	
						80 = {ROOT = { set_character_flag = lost_ambush_bad } }						
						}
					}
					
				
			}
			
		}
		
		
	option = {
		name = DWT970optiona # Wins the fight
		trigger = {
			has_character_flag = won_ambush
		}
			event_target:my_duel_target = {
			random_list = {
				30 = { death = {death_reason = death_battle killer = ROOT } }
				40 = {
					hidden_tooltip = { add_trait = severely_injured }
					}
				30 = {
					hidden_tooltip = { add_trait = wounded}			
					}
				
				}

			}
			ROOT = {
			random_list = {
				20 = {
					hidden_tooltip = { add_trait = severely_injured }
					}
				30 = {
					hidden_tooltip = { add_trait = wounded}			
					hidden_tooltip = {
						random ={
							chance = 40
							add_character_modifier = {
								modifier = black_eye
								months = 10
								}
							}
						}
					}
				
				}

			}
		clr_character_flag = won_ambush
	}
	option = {
		name = DWT970optionb # Loses the fight
		trigger = {
			has_character_flag = lost_ambush
		}
			event_target:my_duel_target = {
			random_list = {
				15 = {
					hidden_tooltip = { add_trait = severely_injured }
					}
				35 = {
					hidden_tooltip = { add_trait = wounded}			
					}
				
				}

			}
			ROOT = {
			random_list = {
				20 = {
					hidden_tooltip = { add_trait = severely_injured }
					}
				30 = {
					hidden_tooltip = { add_trait = wounded}			
					hidden_tooltip = {
						random ={
							chance = 40
							add_character_modifier = {
								modifier = black_eye
								months = 10
								}
							}
						}
 					}
				50 = {
					hidden_tooltip = {
						random ={
							chance = 80
							add_character_modifier = {
								modifier = black_eye
								months = 10
								}
							}
						}
					}
			}
		clr_character_flag = lost_ambush
		}
		hidden_tooltip = { FROM = { narrative_event = { id = DWT.922 } } }
	}
	option = {
		name = DWT970optionc # Loses badly
		trigger = {
			has_character_flag = lost_ambush_bad
		}
			ROOT = {
			random_list = {
				30 = { death = {death_reason = death_battle killer = event_target:my_duel_target } }
				40 = {
					hidden_tooltip = { add_trait = severely_injured }
					hidden_tooltip = {
						random ={
							chance = 40
							add_character_modifier = {
								modifier = black_eye
								months = 10
								}
							}
						}
					}
				30 = {
					hidden_tooltip = { add_trait = wounded}			
					hidden_tooltip = {
						random ={
							chance = 40
							add_character_modifier = {
								modifier = black_eye
								months = 10
								}
							}
						}
					hidden_tooltip = { FROM = { narrative_event = { id = DWT.922 } } }
					}
				
				}
		}
		clr_character_flag = lost_ambush_bad
	}	
	
}


#
### Court rape events that affect a female ruler:
#

# .1990 Random sexual things that can happen while you are in your castle:
narrative_event = {
	id = DWT.1990
	
	ai = no
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		has_rape_content = yes
		prisoner = no
		has_regent = no
		NOT = { trait = incapable }
		in_command = no
		prisoner = no
		is_adult = yes
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 12

		# You got a rapist? Then this will happen more often:
		# UNFINISHED
		#modifier = {
		#	factor = 0.25
		#	owner = { trait = rapist }
		#	FROM = {
		#		ai = no
		#		prisoner = no
		#		in_command = no
		#		practical_age = 16
		#		NOT = { practical_age = 25 }
		#		is_female = yes
		#	}
		#}
		
		# 1.5x the chance of rape if young, either unexperienced or very promiscous.
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			practical_age = 16
			NOT = { practical_age = 25 }
		}
		modifier = { # promiscuous or inexperienced increases this chance
			factor = 0.9
			OR = {
				trait = lilith
				trait = lustful
				trait = hedonist
				trait = cheap_whore
				trait = experienced_whore
				trait = exclusive_whore
				trait = virgin
			}
	
		}
		# 1x the chance of rape if either unexperienced or very promiscous.
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.25
			practical_age = 30
			NOT = { practical_age = 40 }
		}

		# 0.5x the chance of rape if middle aged, unless immortal
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			practical_age = 40
			NOT = {
				practical_age = 50
				}
		}
		modifier = { # very unlikely if old, unless immortal
			factor = 100
			practical_age = 50
		
		
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		random_list = {
		
			# 10% Chances for now. After all, this is a bi-yearly event if the ruler is a stay at home mom!
			10 = { 
				modifier = {
				factor = 10 # if there's already a secret rapist in your court, they're very likely to do it again
					
						any_courtier = {
						OR = {
							has_character_flag = dwt_secret_rapist 
								AND = { 
									trait = rapist
									NOR = { 
										is_lover = ROOT # exclude any lovers
										is_main_spouse = ROOT # exclude your spouse
										is_consort = ROOT # exclude any consorts
										is_female = yes 
									}
								}
							}
						}
					
				
				}
				modifier = { #just to make sure this doesn't fire for males
					factor = 0
					is_female = no
				}
				if = {			#if there's already a secret rapist in the court, we'll have them do it again
					limit = {
						any_courtier = { 
									limit = {
											has_character_flag = dwt_secret_rapist
											prisoner = no
											NOR = { 
												is_female = yes 
												trait = incapable
												trait = infirm
												trait = celibate
												trait = eunuch
												}	
											}
									}
							}
				#they should still be the event target, too, so no need to reassign it, but just to be safe
					save_event_target_as = dwt_secret_rapist
				
			
					}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						any_courtier = { 
									limit = {
											trait = rapist
											prisoner = no
											NOR = { 
												has_character_flag = dwt_false_rape_accusation #if this is the case we're assuming they weren't really a rapist despite the trait
												is_lover = ROOT # exclude any lovers
												is_main_spouse = ROOT # exclude your spouse
												is_consort = ROOT # exclude any consorts
												is_female = yes 
												trait = incapable
												trait = infirm
												trait = celibate
												trait = eunuch
												}	
											}
									}
							}
					save_event_target_as = dwt_secret_rapist
					set_character_flag = dwt_secret_rapist
							
				}
				#otherwise we pick a random courtier
				else = {		
				random_courtier = {
					limit = {
						NOR = { 
							is_lover = ROOT # exclude any lovers
							is_main_spouse = ROOT # exclude your spouse
							is_consort = ROOT # exclude any consorts
							is_female = yes 
							trait = incapable
							trait = infirm
							trait = celibate
							trait = eunuch
							}
						ai = yes #just to make sure we don't somehow select ourselves
						prisoner = no
						is_adult = yes
						}
					save_event_target_as = dwt_secret_rapist
					set_character_flag = dwt_secret_rapist
					if = {
						limit = { #if they had a past false accusation but actually did it this time, we clear that flag just to be safe
							has_character_flag = dwt_false_rape_accusation
							}
						clr_character_flag = dwt_false_rape_accusation
						}
			
					}
				}

				ROOT = { narrative_event = { id = DWT.2000 days = 8 } } 
			} # Raped in your own bed
						
			10 = { ROOT = { narrative_event = { id = DWT.2010 days = 8 } } } # Surprised by your guards
			10 = { 
				modifier = {
					factor = 0
					has_bestiality_content = no				
				}
				ROOT = { narrative_event = { id = DWT.2020 days = 8 } } } # Surprised by a stray dog
			10 = { ROOT = { narrative_event = { id = DWT.2030 days = 8 } } } # Surprised by an Army Commander
			60 = { }
		}
	}
}

narrative_event = {
	id = DWT.2000
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hide_window = yes
	
	trigger = {
		NOT = { trait = futa }
		FROM = {
			ai = no
			prisoner = no
			in_command = no
			is_adult = yes
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					FROM = {
						ai = yes #If the ai somehow triggered this, we simply kill the event
					}
				}
			}
			break = yes
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					is_female = yes
				}
			}
			FROM = {
				narrative_event = { id = DWT.2001} #liege is a female
			}
			break = yes
		}
	}
}

## Female Liege gets surprised by her guards:
narrative_event = {
	id = DWT.2010
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hide_window = yes
	NOT = {
		practical_age = 45
		}	
	trigger = {
		NOT = { trait = futa }
		FROM = {
			ai = no
			prisoner = no
			in_command = no
			is_adult = yes
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					FROM = {
						ai = yes #If the ai somehow triggered this, we simply kill the event
					}
				}
			}
			break = yes
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					is_female = yes
				}
			}
			FROM = {
				narrative_event = { id = DWT.2011} #liege is a female
			}
			break = yes
		}
	}
}

		name = DWT2011option
		hidden_tooltip = { FROM = { narrative_event = { id = DWT.2012 } } }
	}
}

		}

		name = DWT2012optiona

			factor = 100
			}
		}

# 3. Female liege gets surprised by her guards
narrative_event = {	
	id = DWT.2013
	desc = DWT2013desc
	picture = DTW_FL_GuardSurprise3
	
	is_triggered_only = yes	
	
	option = {
		name = DWT2013option
		hidden_tooltip = { FROM = { narrative_event = { id = DWT.2014 } } }
		ROOT = { 
			if = {
				limit = {
					trait = virgin
				}
				remove_trait = virgin 
			}
		}
	}
}

# 4. Female liege gets surprised by her guards
narrative_event = {	
	id = DWT.2014
	desc = DWT2014desc
	picture = DTW_FL_GuardSurprise4
	
	hide_from = yes			# it's a ping back, actually
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = DWT2014option
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		random = { #chance of breaking out of depressed mood
			chance = 10
			remove_trait = depressed
		}

		random = {			# there is 25% chance you'll get lustful
			chance = 25
			add_trait = lustful
		}
		random = {			# there is 5% chance you'll get a memento out of this
			chance = 5
			add_trait = syphilitic
		}
	}
}

## Female Liege gets surprised by a stray dog:
narrative_event = {
	id = DWT.2020
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hide_window = yes
	
	trigger = {
		NOT = { trait = futa }
		FROM = {
			ai = no
			prisoner = no
			in_command = no
			is_adult = yes
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					FROM = {
						ai = yes #If the ai somehow triggered this, we simply kill the event
					}
				}
			}
			break = yes
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					is_female = yes
				}
			}
			FROM = {
				narrative_event = { id = DWT.2021} #liege is a female
			}
			break = yes
		}
	}
}

#
### Female Liege gets surprised by an Army Commander
#

narrative_event = {
	id = DWT.2030
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hide_window = yes
	
	trigger = {
		NOT = { trait = futa }
		FROM = {
			ai = no
			prisoner = no
			in_command = no
			is_adult = yes
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					FROM = {
						ai = yes #If the ai somehow triggered this, we simply kill the event
					}
				}
			}
			break = yes
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					is_female = yes
				}
			}
			FROM = {
				narrative_event = { id = DWT.951} #liege is a female
			}
			break = yes
		}
	}
}

## End - Female Liege gets surprised by an Army Commander

# Culprit discovered
narrative_event = {
	id = DWT.2090
	desc = DWT2090desc
	picture = DWTArrest
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
	clear_event_target = event_target:dwt_rape_investigator
	}
	
	option = { # throw in jail
		name = DWT2090optiona
		event_target:dwt_secret_rapist = { 
		imprison = ROOT
		add_trait = rapist
		}
		ROOT = {
					opinion = {								
				modifier = opinion_raped_me
				who = event_target:dwt_secret_rapist
			}
		clear_event_target = event_target:dwt_secret_rapist

		}
	}
	option = { #banish
		name = DWT2090optionb
		event_target:dwt_secret_rapist = { 
		add_trait = rapist
		banish = yes
		}
		ROOT = {
					opinion = {								
				modifier = opinion_raped_me
				who = event_target:dwt_secret_rapist
			}
		clear_event_target = event_target:dwt_secret_rapist

		}
		
	
	}
	option = { #summary execution
		name = DWT2090optionc
		event_target:dwt_secret_rapist = { 
		add_trait = rapist
		death = {death_reason = death_execution killer = ROOT }		
		}
		ROOT = {
				if = {
					limit = { trait = just }
					random = {
						chance = 40
						remove_trait = just
						}
					}
				else = {
					random = {
						chance = 40
						add_trait = arbitrary
						}
					}
			}



	}
}

# .3000 Male ruler decides to rape female prisoner and chooses what to do with her:
narrative_event = {
	id = DWT.3000
	desc = DWT.3000.desc
	
	picture = DWTHarleyClothedPrisonerGeneric2
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		event_target:is_rape_victim = { character = yes } # 

	}
	
	# Vaginal rape decission:
	option = { 
		trigger = {
			event_target:is_rape_victim = { character = yes } # 
		}
		name = DWT.3000.vaginal
		event_target:is_rape_victim = {
			prestige = -15
			piety = -5
			# Piss off their entire dynasty, too:
			if = {
				limit = { 
					event_target:is_rape_victim = { 
						NOT = { dynasty = event_target:is_rapist } 
					}
				}
				liege = {									# Piss off their liege (a little):
					opinion = {
						modifier = opinion_raped_subject
						who = event_target:is_rapist
					}
					prestige = -1
					piety = -2
				}
				any_dynasty_member = {
					limit = { NOT = { character = event_target:is_rape_victim } }
					opinion = {
						modifier = opinion_raped_family
						who = event_target:is_rapist
					}
					prestige = -5
					piety = -3
				}
				spouse = { 
					opinion = {
						modifier = opinion_raped_spouse
						who = event_target:is_rapist
					}
				}
				prestige = -15
				piety = -5
				clr_character_flag  = victim_lost_brawl # As we start fresh, victim should *not* (yet) have this flag anyway.
			}			
		}
		event_target:is_rapist = { 					# calling the character event, you're the scope
			prestige = 5
			piety = -15
		}
		narrative_event = { id = DWT.3010 } 
	}
	# Anal rape decission:
	option = { 
		trigger = {
			event_target:is_rape_victim = { character = yes } # 
		}
		name = DWT.3000.anal
		event_target:is_rape_victim = {
			prestige = -10
			piety = -10
			# Piss off their entire dynasty, too:
			if = {
				limit = { 
					event_target:is_rape_victim = { 
						NOT = { dynasty = event_target:is_rapist } 
					}
				}
				liege = {									# Piss off their liege (a little):
					opinion = {
						modifier = opinion_raped_subject
						who = event_target:is_rapist
					}
					prestige = -1
					piety = -2
				}
				any_dynasty_member = {
					limit = { NOT = { character = event_target:is_rape_victim } } 
					opinion = {
						modifier = opinion_raped_family
						who = event_target:is_rapist
					}
					prestige = -5
					piety = -10
				}
				spouse = { 
					opinion = {
						modifier = opinion_raped_spouse
						who = event_target:is_rapist
					}
				}
				prestige = -5
				piety = -10
				
				clr_character_flag  = victim_lost_brawl
			}
		}
		event_target:is_rapist = { 					# calling the character event, you're the scope
			prestige = 5
			piety = -15
		}
		narrative_event = { id = DWT.3020 }
	}

	# Oral rape decission:
	option = { 
		trigger = {
			event_target:is_rape_victim = { character = yes } # 
		}
		name = DWT.3000.oral
		event_target:is_rape_victim = {
			prestige = -5
			piety = -1
			# Piss off their entire dynasty, too:
			if = {
				limit = { 
					event_target:is_rape_victim = { 
						NOT = { dynasty = event_target:is_rapist } 
					}
				}
				liege = {									# Piss off their liege (a little):
					opinion = {
						modifier = opinion_raped_subject
						who = event_target:is_rapist
					}
					prestige = -1
					piety = -2
				}
				any_dynasty_member = {
					limit = { NOT = { character = event_target:is_rape_victim } }
					opinion = {
						modifier = opinion_raped_family
						who = event_target:is_rapist
					}
					prestige = -5
					piety = -1
				}
				spouse = { 
					opinion = {
						modifier = opinion_raped_spouse
						who = event_target:is_rapist
					}
				}
				prestige = -5
				piety = -1
				clr_character_flag  = victim_lost_brawl
			}			
		}
		event_target:is_rapist = { 					# calling the character event, you're the scope
			prestige = 5
			piety = -15
		}
		narrative_event = { id = DWT.3030 }
	}
	# Nah, just kidding:
	option = { 
		trigger = {
			event_target:is_rape_victim = { character = yes } # 
		}
		name = DWT.3000.kidding
		event_target:is_rape_victim = {
			opinion = {				# She will hate that she was at your mercy.
				modifier = opinion_almost_raped_me
				who = event_target:is_rapist
			}
			piety = 10 # Quite a religious experience. See? Prayers work! (just kidding)
			clr_character_flag = rape_target
		}
		event_target:is_rapist = { 					# calling the character event, you're the scope
			piety = 5 # Live and let live. You made a choice that pleases god.
			clr_character_flag = raping_prisoner
		}
	}
}

# The victim is brave, strong, shrewd or lunatic enough to fight back - fight #1:
narrative_event = { 
	id = DWT.3002
	desc = DWT.3002.desc
	picture = RedSonjaWithKnife

	is_triggered_only = yes

	# Resistance to rape: Victim flees
	option = { 
		trigger = {
			event_target:is_rape_victim = { character = yes } # 

		}

		name = DWTRapeFemaleFleesFightHer
		event_target:is_rape_victim = {
			opinion = {								# Although she wasn't raped, she will hate you more in the next few days with the rape attempt fresh on her mind
				modifier = opinion_rape_fight
				who = event_target:is_rapist
			}
			piety = 10 								# Quite a religious experience. See? Prayers work! (just kidding)
			random = {								# There is 15% chance she'll be wounded
				chance = 15
				add_trait = wounded
			}
		}
		event_target:is_rapist = { 					# calling the character event, you're the scope
			opinion = {								# Funny, isn't it?
				modifier = dw_opinion_mildly_entertained 
				who = event_target:is_rape_victim
			}

			random = {								# There is 15% chance you'll be wounded
				chance = 15
				add_trait = wounded
			}
		}
		# Fight ensues:
		#FROMliege = { narrative_event = { id = DWT.3003 } }
		narrative_event = { id = DWT.3003 }
	}
	# Let her go:

		trigger = {
			event_target:is_rape_victim = { character = yes } # 
		}
		name = DWTRapeFemaleFleesEscapeTolerated
		event_target:is_rape_victim = {
			opinion = {				# She will hate that she was at your mercy.
				modifier = opinion_almost_raped_me
				who = event_target:is_rapist

			clr_character_flag = rape_target
			random = {								# There is 25% chance she'll be wounded
				chance = 25
				add_trait = wounded
			}
		}
		event_target:is_rapist = { 					# calling the character event, you're the scope
			opinion = {								# You're amused.
				modifier = dw_opinion_mildly_entertained 
				who = event_target:is_rape_victim
			}

				add_trait = wounded

# The victim is brave, strong, shrewd or lunatic enough to fight back - fight - you win or loose #2:
narrative_event = { 
	id = DWT.3003
	hide_window = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		event_target:is_rape_victim = { character = yes }

	}

	# Determine how the fight goes:
	immediate = {
		random_list = {		
			25 = { #80%
				# Rapist wins and proceeds with violent rape:
				# For this we mark the victim as having lost the brawl:
				event_target:is_rape_victim = { set_character_flag = victim_lost_brawl }
				narrative_event = { id = DWT.3004 }
			} 
			25 = { #9%
				# Rapist wins, but victim dies:
				narrative_event = { id = DWT.3005 }
			} 
			25 = { #10%
				# Victim wins and flees:
				narrative_event = { id = DWT.3006 }
			} 
			25 = { #1%
				# Victim wins and rapist dies:
				narrative_event = { id = DWT.3007 }
			} 
		}
	}	
}

# Victim lost fight and we continue with what we had in mind:
narrative_event = { 
	id = DWT.3004
	desc = DWT.3004.desc
	picture = DWTHarleyBloodBatKill

	is_triggered_only = yes

	# When we get here we lost the scope and need to reacquire it again. That's why we set flags:
	immediate = {
		if = { # Grab Victim if available:
			limit = {
				location = {
					any_province_character = {
						has_character_flag = victim_lost_brawl
						ai = yes
					}
				}
			}
			# If there is, we then grab the Victim for the event
			location = {
				random_province_character = {
					limit = {
						has_character_flag = victim_lost_brawl
						ai = yes
					}
					save_event_target_as = is_rape_victim
				}
			}
		}
		if = { # Grab Rapist if available:
			limit = {
				location = {
					any_province_character = {
						has_character_flag = raping_prisoner
						ai = no
					}
				}
			}
			# If there is, we then grab the Rapist for the event
			location = {
				random_province_character = {
					limit = {
						has_character_flag = raping_prisoner
						ai = no
					}
					save_event_target_as = is_rapist
				}
			}
		}
	}
		
	option = { 
		trigger = {
			has_character_flag = victim_lost_brawl
			event_target:is_rape_victim = { character = yes } # 
		}
		name = DWToptionNowYouReMine
		event_target:is_rape_victim = {
			remove_trait = honest
			add_trait = deceitful
			opinion = {								# She will hate you for a looooong time.
				modifier = opinion_raped_me
				who = event_target:is_rapist
			}
		}
		event_target:is_rapist = { 					# calling the character event, you're the scope
			opinion = {								# She refused your 'gift' (you only had her 'best' in mind) and that upsets you. You know: Because ... stupid reasons!
				modifier = opinion_ungrateful 
				who = event_target:is_rape_victim
			}
		}
		narrative_event = { id = DWT.3008 } 			# Back to step 1 as we proceed as initially planned, but this time more violent (poor thing!)
	}
}

#### The acts:
# Vaginal rape of female through male liege - act #1
narrative_event = { 
	id = DWT.3010
	desc = DWT.3010.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_DWT.rapevag1

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { 
		trigger = {
			event_target:is_rape_victim = { character = yes } # 
		}
		name = DWToptionfurther
		event_target:is_rape_victim = {
			if = {
				limit = { 			# if victim is a recognised virgin, you ruin her virginhood, and she will hate you even more
					trait = virgin 
				}
				remove_trait = virgin
				prestige = -5
				piety = -10
				opinion = {
					modifier = opinion_took_virginity_by_force
					who = event_target:is_rapist
				}
				any_dynasty_member = {
					limit = { NOT = { dynasty = event_target:is_rape_victim } }
					opinion = {
						modifier = opinion_took_family_members_virginity_by_force
						who = event_target:is_rapist
					}
					prestige = -5
					piety = -10
				}
				spouse = { 
					opinion = {
						modifier = opinion_took_family_members_virginity_by_force
						who = event_target:is_rapist
					}
					prestige = -5
					piety = -10
				}
				event_target:is_rapist = {
					prestige = 15
					piety = -10
				}
			}
			add_trait = raped		# mark the victim as raped
		}
		event_target:is_rapist = { 	# calling the character event, you're the scope
			add_trait = rapist
			random = {
				chance = 25			
				add_trait = proud
			}
			if = {
				limit = { 			# if you are a recognised virgin we remove this trait:
					trait = virgin 
				}
				remove_trait = virgin
			}
		}
		narrative_event = { id = DWT.3011 }
	}
}

# Vaginal rape of female through male liege - act #3
narrative_event = { 
	id =  DWT.3012
	desc = DWT.3112.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_DWT.rapevag3

	is_triggered_only = yes

	# Creampie:
	option = { 
		trigger = {
			event_target:is_rape_victim = { character = yes } # 
		}
		name = DWTRapeDoCreampie
		event_target:is_rape_victim = {
			opinion = {								# She will hate you
				modifier = raper_ruler
				who = event_target:is_rapist
			}
			hidden_tooltip = {
				character_event = { id = 9000 } # check for pregnancy

			}
		}
		event_target:is_rape_victim = { change_learning = 1 impregnate = event_target:is_rapist }
		if = {
			limit = {
				event_target:is_rapist = {
					trait = yiminhyee
				}
				event_target:is_rape_victim = {
					is_female = yes
				}
			}
			event_target:is_rape_victim = { 
				impregnate_cuckoo = event_target:is_rapist
				change_learning = 1
			}
		}
		narrative_event = { id = DWT.3013 }
	}
	# Pull out:
	option = { 
		trigger = {
			event_target:is_rape_victim = { character = yes } # 
		}
		name = DWTRapeNoCreampie
		event_target:is_rape_victim = {
			opinion = {								# She will hate you more in the next few days with the rape fresh on her mind
				modifier = raper_ruler
				who = event_target:is_rapist
			}
		}
		event_target:is_rapist = { 					# calling the character event, you're the scope
			}
			opinion = {								# Oh, you had your fun with her!
				modifier = dw_opinion_good_fuck
				who = event_target:is_rape_victim
			}
			add_character_modifier = { name = dw_good_sex duration = 30 }
		
		narrative_event = { id = DWT.3014 }
	}
}

				who = event_target:is_rapist

			clr_character_flag = rape_target
		}

				modifier = dw_opinion_good_fuck
				who = event_target:is_rape_victim

# Victim lost too much health during the rape and dies:
narrative_event = { 
	id = DWT.3040
	desc = DWT.3040.desc
	picture = DWTHarleyBloodFace

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		event_target:is_rape_victim = { character = yes }
		event_target:is_rape_victim = { NOT = { health = 0.1 } }
	}
	
	option = { 
		trigger = {
			event_target:is_rape_victim = { character = yes }
			#event_target:is_rape_victim = { NOT = { health = 0.1 } }
		}
		name = DWToptionRapeVictimDies
		event_target:is_rape_victim = { 
			clr_character_flag = victim_lost_brawl
			clr_character_flag = rape_target
			death = { death_reason = dwt_death_rape_prisoner } 
			any_dynasty_member = {
				limit = { NOT = { character = event_target:is_rape_victim } }
				opinion = {
					modifier = opinion_killed_close_kin
					who = event_target:is_rapist
				}
				prestige = -5
				piety = -1
			}
			father = { 
				opinion = {
					modifier = opinion_executed_child
					who = event_target:is_rapist
				}
			}
			mother = { 
				opinion = {
					modifier = opinion_executed_child
					who = event_target:is_rapist
				}
			}
			spouse = { 
				opinion = {
					modifier = opinion_spouse_slayer
					who = event_target:is_rapist
				}
			}
			any_child = {
				opinion = {
					modifier = opinion_killed_close_kin
					who = event_target:is_rapist
				}			
			}
		}
		event_target:is_rapist = { 					# calling the character event, you're the scope
			clr_character_flag = raping_prisoner
		}
		# Done!
	}
}

# .3100 Male ruler decides to rape female courtier and chooses what to do with her:
narrative_event = {
	id = DWT.3100
	desc = DWT.3100.desc
	
	picture = DWTHarleyBloodyDamselinDistress
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		event_target:is_rape_victim = { character = yes } # 
			
	}
	
	# Vaginal rape decission:
	option = { 
		trigger = {
			event_target:is_rape_victim = { character = yes } # 
		}
		name = DWT.3100.vaginal
		event_target:is_rape_victim = {
			prestige = -15
			piety = -5
			# Piss off their entire dynasty, too:
			if = {
				limit = { 
					event_target:is_rape_victim = { 
						NOT = { dynasty = event_target:is_rapist } 
					}
				}
				liege = {									# Piss off their liege (a little):
					opinion = {
						modifier = opinion_raped_subject
						who = event_target:is_rapist
					}
					prestige = -1
					piety = -2
				}
				any_dynasty_member = {
					limit = { NOT = { character = event_target:is_rape_victim } }
					opinion = {
						modifier = opinion_raped_family
						who = event_target:is_rapist
					}
					prestige = -5
					piety = -3
				}
				spouse = { 
					opinion = {
						modifier = opinion_raped_spouse
						who = event_target:is_rapist
					}
				}
				prestige = -15
				piety = -5
				clr_character_flag  = victim_lost_brawl # As we start fresh, victim should *not* (yet) have this flag anyway.
			}			
		}

					}

				prestige = -5

# The victim is brave, strong, shrewd or lunatic enough to fight back - fight #1:
narrative_event = { 
	id = DWT.3102
	desc = DWT.3102.desc
	picture = DWTManWomanSwordFight

	is_triggered_only = yes

	# Resistance to rape: Victim flees
	option = { 
		trigger = {
			event_target:is_rape_victim = { character = yes } # 
		}

		name = DWTRapeFemaleFleesFightHer
		event_target:is_rape_victim = {
			opinion = {								# Although she wasn't raped, she will hate you more in the next few days with the rape attempt fresh on her mind
				modifier = opinion_rape_fight
				who = event_target:is_rapist
			}
			piety = 10 								# Quite a religious experience. See? Prayers work! (just kidding)
			random = {								# There is 15% chance she'll be wounded
				chance = 15
				add_trait = wounded
			}
		}
		event_target:is_rapist = { 					# calling the character event, you're the scope
			opinion = {								# Funny, isn't it?
				modifier = dw_opinion_mildly_entertained 
				who = event_target:is_rape_victim
			}
			piety = -5 								# There is a price for everything.
			random = {								# There is 15% chance you'll be wounded
				chance = 15
				add_trait = wounded
			}
		}
		# Fight ensues:
		#FROMFROM = { narrative_event = { id = DWT.3103 } }
		narrative_event = { id = DWT.3103 }
	}
	# Let her go:
	option = { 
		trigger = {
			event_target:is_rape_victim = { character = yes } # 
		}
		name = DWTRapeFemaleFleesEscapeTolerated
		event_target:is_rape_victim = {
			opinion = {				# She will hate that she was at your mercy.
				modifier = opinion_almost_raped_me
				who = event_target:is_rapist
			}
			piety = 10 								# Quite a religious experience. See? Prayers work! (just kidding)
			clr_character_flag = rape_target
			random = {								# There is 25% chance she'll be wounded
				chance = 25
				add_trait = wounded
			}

			# Check if rapist is asocial:
			if = {
				limit = {
					event_target:is_rapist = {
						trait = asocial
					}
				}
				health = -2.5
				opinion = {
					modifier = opinion_raped_me2
					who = event_target:is_rapist
				}
			}
		}
		event_target:is_rapist = { 					# calling the character event, you're the scope
			opinion = {								# You're amused.
				modifier = dw_opinion_mildly_entertained 
				who = event_target:is_rape_victim
			}
			piety = 5 # Live and let live. You made a choice that pleases god.
			clr_character_flag = raping_courtier
			random = {								# There is 25% chance you'll be wounded
				chance = 25
				add_trait = wounded
			}
		}
		narrative_event = { id = DWT.3140 }	# Done - end of chain, check if she dies
	}

# The victim is brave, strong, shrewd or lunatic enough to fight back - fight - you win or loose #2:

	is_triggered_only = yes

	}

	immediate = {
		random_list = {		
			80 = { 
				# Rapist wins and proceeds with violent rape:
				# For this we mark the victim as having lost the brawl:
				event_target:is_rape_victim = { set_character_flag = victim_lost_brawl }
				narrative_event = { id = DWT.3104 }
			} 
			09 = { 
				# Rapist wins, but victim dies:
				narrative_event = { id = DWT.3105 }
			} 
			10 = { 
				# Victim wins and flees:
				narrative_event = { id = DWT.3106 }
			} 
			01 = { 
				# Victim wins and rapist dies:
				narrative_event = { id = DWT.3107 }
			} 
		}
	}	
}

# Victim lost fight and we continue with what we had in mind:
narrative_event = { 
	id = DWT.3104
	desc = DWT.3104.desc
	picture = DWTHarleyBloodBatKill

	is_triggered_only = yes

	# When we get here we lost the scope and need to reacquire it again. That's why we set flags:
	immediate = {
		if = { # Grab Victim if available:
			limit = {
				location = {
					any_province_character = {
						has_character_flag = victim_lost_brawl
						ai = yes
					}
				}
			}
			# If there is, we then grab the Victim for the event
			location = {
				random_province_character = {
					limit = {
						has_character_flag = victim_lost_brawl
						ai = yes
					}
					save_event_target_as = is_rape_victim
				}
			}
		}
		if = { # Grab Rapist if available:
			limit = {
				location = {
					any_province_character = {
						has_character_flag = raping_courtier
						ai = no
					}
				}
			}
			# If there is, we then grab the Rapist for the event
			location = {
				random_province_character = {
					limit = {
						has_character_flag = raping_courtier
						ai = no
					}
					save_event_target_as = is_rapist
				}
			}
		}
	}
		
	option = { 
		trigger = {
			has_character_flag = victim_lost_brawl
			event_target:is_rape_victim = { character = yes } # 
		}
		name = DWToptionNowYouReMine
		event_target:is_rape_victim = {
			remove_trait = honest
			add_trait = deceitful
			opinion = {								# She will hate you for a looooong time.
				modifier = immortal_hate
				who = event_target:is_rapist
			}
		}
		event_target:is_rapist = { 					# calling the character event, you're the scope
			opinion = {								# She refused your 'gift' (you only had her 'best' in mind) and that upsets you. You know: Because ... stupid reasons!
				modifier = opinion_ungrateful 
				who = event_target:is_rape_victim
			}
		}
		narrative_event = { id = DWT.3108 } 			# Back to step 1 as we proceed as initially planned, but this time more violent (poor thing!)
	}
}

				}

				}			
			}
		}
		event_target:is_rapist = { 					# calling the character event, you're the scope

#### The acts:
# Vaginal rape of female courtier through male liege - act #1
narrative_event = { 
	id = DWT.3110
	desc = DWT.3110.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_DWT.sexvag1

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { 
		trigger = {
			event_target:is_rape_victim = { character = yes } # 
			
		}
		name = DWToptionfurther
		event_target:is_rape_victim = {
			if = {
				limit = { 			# if victim is a recognised virgin, you ruin her virginhood, and she will hate you even more
					trait = virgin 
				}
				remove_trait = virgin
				prestige = -5
				piety = -10
				opinion = {
					modifier = opinion_took_virginity_by_force
					who = event_target:is_rapist
				}
				any_dynasty_member = {
					limit = { NOT = { dynasty = event_target:is_rape_victim } }
					opinion = {
						modifier = opinion_took_family_members_virginity_by_force
						who = event_target:is_rapist
					}
					prestige = -5
					piety = -10
				}
				spouse = { 
					opinion = {
						modifier = opinion_took_family_members_virginity_by_force
						who = event_target:is_rapist
					}
					prestige = -5
					piety = -10
				}
				event_target:is_rapist = {
					prestige = 15
					piety = -10
				}
			}
			add_trait = raped		# mark the victim as raped
		}
		event_target:is_rapist = { 	# calling the character event, you're the scope
			add_trait = rapist
			random = {
				chance = 25			
				add_trait = proud
			}
			if = {
				limit = { 			# if you are a recognised virgin we remove this trait:
					trait = virgin 
				}
				remove_trait = virgin
			}
		}
		narrative_event = { id = DWT.3111 }
	}
}

narrative_event = { 
	id =  DWT.3112
	desc = DWT.3112.desc
	picture = DWTMFFCreampie

	is_triggered_only = yes

	# Creampie:
	option = { 
		trigger = {
			event_target:is_rape_victim = { character = yes } # 
		}

		event_target:is_rape_victim = {
			opinion = {								# She will hate you
				modifier = raper_ruler
				who = event_target:is_rapist
			}
			hidden_tooltip = {
				character_event = { id = 9000 } # check for pregnancy

			}

		}
		event_target:is_rapist = { 					# calling the character event, you're the scope
			
			opinion = {								# Oh, you had your fun with her!
				modifier = dw_opinion_good_fuck
				who = event_target:is_rape_victim
			}
			add_character_modifier = { name = dw_good_sex duration = 30 }
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				event_target:is_rapist = {
					trait = yiminhyee
				}
				event_target:is_rape_victim = {
					is_female = yes
				}
			}
			event_target:is_rape_victim = { 
				impregnate_cuckoo = event_target:is_rapist
				change_learning = 1
			}
		}
		narrative_event = { id = DWT.3113 }
	}
	# Pull out:
	option = { 
		trigger = {
			event_target:is_rape_victim = { character = yes } # 
		}
		name = DWTRapeNoCreampie
		event_target:is_rape_victim = {
			opinion = {								# She will hate you more in the next few days with the rape fresh on her mind
				modifier = raper_ruler
				who = event_target:is_rapist
			}
		}
		event_target:is_rapist = { 					# calling the character event, you're the scope
			
			opinion = {								# Oh, you had your fun with her!
				modifier = dw_opinion_good_fuck
				who = event_target:is_rape_victim
			}
			add_character_modifier = { name = dw_good_sex duration = 30 }
		}
		narrative_event = { id = DWT.3114 }
	}
}

				}
			}
		}
		event_target:is_rapist = { 					# calling the character event, you're the scope
			opinion = {								# Oh, you had your fun with her!
				modifier = dw_opinion_good_fuck
				who = event_target:is_rape_victim
			}

			random = {
				chance = 25			
				add_trait = proud
			}
			if = {
				limit = { 			# if you are a recognised virgin we remove this trait:
					trait = virgin 
				}
				remove_trait = virgin
			}
		}
		narrative_event = { id = DWT.3121 }
	}
}

# Victim courtier lost too much health during the rape and dies:
narrative_event = { 
	id = DWT.3140
	desc = DWT.3140.desc
	picture = DWTHarleyGirlFeet

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		event_target:is_rape_victim = { character = yes }
		event_target:is_rape_victim = { NOT = { health = 0.1 } }
	}
	
	option = { 
		trigger = {
			event_target:is_rape_victim = { character = yes }
			#event_target:is_rape_victim = { NOT = { health = 0.1 } }
		}
		name = DWToptionRapeVictimDies
		event_target:is_rape_victim = { 
			clr_character_flag = victim_lost_brawl
			clr_character_flag = rape_target
			death = { death_reason = dwt_death_rape_courtier } 
			any_dynasty_member = {
				limit = { NOT = { character = event_target:is_rape_victim } }
				opinion = {
					modifier = opinion_killed_close_kin
					who = event_target:is_rapist
				}
				prestige = -5
				piety = -1
			}
			father = { 
				opinion = {
					modifier = opinion_executed_child
					who = event_target:is_rapist
				}
			}
			mother = { 
				opinion = {
					modifier = opinion_executed_child
					who = event_target:is_rapist
				}
			}
			spouse = { 
				opinion = {
					modifier = opinion_spouse_slayer
					who = event_target:is_rapist
				}
			}
			any_child = {
				opinion = {
					modifier = opinion_killed_close_kin
					who = event_target:is_rapist
				}			
			}
		}
		event_target:is_rapist = { 					# calling the character event, you're the scope
			clr_character_flag = raping_courtier
		}
		# Done!
	}
}

## End: New extended event chain for male ruler rapes female courtier.

# .3200 Male ruler has consensual sex with a willing woman and chooses what to do with her:
narrative_event = {
	id = DWT.3200
	desc = DWT.3200.desc
	
	picture = DTW_FL_GuardSurprise1
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		event_target:is_lustful_participant = { character = yes } # 
	}
	
	# Vaginal act decission:
	option = { 
		trigger = {
			event_target:is_lustful_participant = { character = yes } # 
		}
		name = DWT.3200.vaginal
		event_target:is_lustful_participant = {
			prestige = 15
			piety = 5
			# Piss off their entire dynasty, too:
			if = {
				limit = { 
					event_target:is_lustful_participant = { 
						NOT = { dynasty = event_target:is_rapist } 
					}
				}
				any_dynasty_member = {
					limit = { NOT = { character = event_target:is_lustful_participant } }
					opinion = {
						modifier = opinion_used_family_member
						who = event_target:is_rapist
					}
					prestige = -5
					piety = -3
				}
				spouse = { 
					opinion = {
						modifier = opinion_used_spouse
						who = event_target:is_rapist
					}
				}
				prestige = -15
				piety = -5
				clr_character_flag  = victim_lost_brawl # As we start fresh, victim should *not* (yet) have this flag anyway.
			}			
		}
		event_target:is_rapist = { 					# calling the character event, you're the scope
			prestige = 5
			piety = -15
		}
		narrative_event = { id = DWT.3210 }

# Vaginal sex with willing female courtier and male liege - act #1
narrative_event = { 
	id = DWT.3210
	desc = DWT.3210.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_DWT.sexvag1

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { 
		trigger = {
			event_target:is_lustful_participant = { character = yes } # 
		}
		name = DWToptionfurther
		event_target:is_lustful_participant = {
			if = {
				limit = { 			# if victim is a recognised virgin, you ruin her virginhood, and she will hate you even more
					trait = virgin 
				}
				remove_trait = virgin
				prestige = -1
				piety = -3
				opinion = {
					modifier = opinion_took_virginity
					who = event_target:is_rapist
				}
				spouse = { 
					opinion = {
						modifier = opinion_took_family_members_virginity_by_force		# Because this is the spouse. So it must have been rape in their eyes, right?
						who = event_target:is_rapist
					}
					prestige = -5
					piety = -10
				}
				event_target:is_rapist = {
					prestige = 15
					piety = -10
				}
			}
		}
		event_target:is_rapist = { 	# calling the character event, you're the scope
			if = {
				limit = { 			# if you are a recognised virgin we remove this trait:
					trait = virgin 
				}
				remove_trait = virgin
			}
		}
		narrative_event = { id = DWT.3211 }
	}
}

# Vaginal sex with willing female courtier and male liege - act #3
narrative_event = { 
	id =  DWT.3212
	desc = DWT.3212.desc
	picture = DWTMFFCreampie

	is_triggered_only = yes

	# Creampie:
	option = { 
		trigger = {
			event_target:is_lustful_participant = { character = yes } # 
		}
		name = DWTRapeDoCreampie
		event_target:is_lustful_participant = {
			opinion = {								# Because we're a mysogonist we assume that she liked it, too.
				modifier = dw_opinion_good_fuck
				who = event_target:is_rapist
			}
			add_character_modifier = { name = dw_good_sex duration = 30 }
			if = { 
				limit = {							# if victim under 40 and not pregnant, 25% chance to get pregnant
					NOT = { practical_age = 40 }
					is_pregnant = no
					fertility = 0.5
				}
				random = { 
					chance = 25
					impregnate = event_target:is_rapist
				}
			}
		}
		event_target:is_rapist = { 					# calling the character event, you're the scope
			if = {
				limit = { trait = weak } 
				random = {
					chance = 10
					remove_trait = weak
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { trait = strong } }
				random = {
					chance = 5
					add_trait = strong
					remove_trait = weak
				}
			}
		}
		narrative_event = { id = DWT.3213 }
	}
	# Pull out:
	option = { 
		trigger = {
			event_target:is_lustful_participant = { character = yes } # 
		}
		name = DWTRapeNoCreampie
		event_target:is_lustful_participant = {
			opinion = {								# Because we're a mysogonist we assume that she liked it, too.
				modifier = dw_opinion_good_fuck
				who = event_target:is_rapist
			}
		}
		event_target:is_rapist = { 					# calling the character event, you're the scope
			if = {
				limit = { trait = weak } 
				random = {
					chance = 10
					remove_trait = weak
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { trait = strong } }
				random = {
					chance = 5
					add_trait = strong
					remove_trait = weak
				}
			}
			opinion = {								# Oh, you had your fun with her!
				modifier = dw_opinion_good_fuck
				who = event_target:is_lustful_participant
			}
			add_character_modifier = { name = dw_good_sex duration = 30 }
		}
		narrative_event = { id = DWT.3214 }
	}
}

# .3300 Male ruler decides to rape male prisoner and chooses what to do with him:
narrative_event = {
	id = DWT.3300
	desc = DWT.3300.desc
	
	picture = DWTPrisonerShirtlessHandsBound
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
			
		event_target:is_rape_victim = { character = yes } # 
	}
	
	# Anal rape decission:
	option = { 
		trigger = {
			event_target:is_rape_victim = { character = yes } # 
		}
		name = DWT.3300.anal
		event_target:is_rape_victim = {
			prestige = -10
			piety = -10
			# Piss off their entire dynasty, too:
			if = {
				limit = { 
					event_target:is_rape_victim = { 
						NOT = { dynasty = event_target:is_rapist } 
					}
				}
				liege = {									# Piss off their liege (a little):
					opinion = {
						modifier = opinion_raped_subject
						who = event_target:is_rapist
					}
					prestige = -1
					piety = -2
				}
				any_dynasty_member = {
					limit = { NOT = { character = event_target:is_rape_victim } } 
					opinion = {
						modifier = opinion_raped_family
						who = event_target:is_rapist
					}
					prestige = -5
					piety = -10
				}
				spouse = { 
					opinion = {
						modifier = opinion_raped_spouse
						who = event_target:is_rapist
					}
				}
				prestige = -5
				piety = -10
				
				clr_character_flag  = victim_lost_brawl
			}
		}
		event_target:is_rapist = { 					# calling the character event, you're the scope
			prestige = 5
			piety = -15
		}
		narrative_event = { id = DWT.3320 }
	}
	# Nah, just kidding:
	option = { 
		trigger = {
			event_target:is_rape_victim = { character = yes } # 
		}
		name = DWT.3300.kidding
		event_target:is_rape_victim = {
			opinion = {				# She will hate that she was at your mercy.
				modifier = opinion_almost_raped_me
				who = event_target:is_rapist
			}
			piety = 10 # Quite a religious experience. See? Prayers work! (just kidding)
			clr_character_flag = rape_target
		}
		event_target:is_rapist = { 					# calling the character event, you're the scope
			piety = 5 # Live and let live. You made a choice that pleases god.
			clr_character_flag = raping_prisoner
		}
	}
}

# The victim is brave, strong, shrewd or lunatic enough to fight back - fight - you win or loose #2:
narrative_event = { 
	id = DWT.3303
	hide_window = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		event_target:is_rape_victim = { character = yes }
	}

	# Determine how the fight goes:
	immediate = {
		random_list = {		
			25 = { #80%
				# Rapist wins and proceeds with violent rape:
				# For this we mark the victim as having lost the brawl:
				event_target:is_rape_victim = { set_character_flag = victim_lost_brawl }
				narrative_event = { id = DWT.3304 }
			} 
			25 = { #9%
				# Rapist wins, but victim dies:
				narrative_event = { id = DWT.3305 }
			} 
			25 = { #10%
				# Victim wins and flees:
				narrative_event = { id = DWT.3306 }
			} 
			25 = { #1%
				# Victim wins and rapist dies:
				narrative_event = { id = DWT.3307 }
			} 
		}
	}	
}

# Victim lost fight and we continue with what we had in mind:
narrative_event = { 
	id = DWT.3304
	desc = DWT.3304.desc
	picture = DWTPrisonerShirtlessHandsBound

	is_triggered_only = yes

	# When we get here we lost the scope and need to reacquire it again. That's why we set flags:
	immediate = {
		if = { # Grab Victim if available:
			limit = {
				location = {
					any_province_character = {
						has_character_flag = victim_lost_brawl
						ai = yes
					}
				}
			}
			# If there is, we then grab the Victim for the event
			location = {
				random_province_character = {
					limit = {
						has_character_flag = victim_lost_brawl
						ai = yes
					}
					save_event_target_as = is_rape_victim
				}
			}
		}
		if = { # Grab Rapist if available:
			limit = {
				location = {
					any_province_character = {
						has_character_flag = raping_prisoner
						ai = no
					}
				}
			}
			# If there is, we then grab the Rapist for the event
			location = {
				random_province_character = {
					limit = {
						has_character_flag = raping_prisoner
						ai = no
					}
					save_event_target_as = is_rapist
				}
			}
		}
	}
		
	option = { 
		trigger = {
			has_character_flag = victim_lost_brawl
			event_target:is_rape_victim = { character = yes } # 
		}
		name = DWToptionNowYouReMine
		event_target:is_rape_victim = {
			remove_trait = honest
			add_trait = deceitful
			opinion = {								# She will hate you for a looooong time.
				modifier = immortal_hate
				who = event_target:is_rapist
			}
		}
		event_target:is_rapist = { 					# calling the character event, you're the scope
			opinion = {								# She refused your 'gift' (you only had her 'best' in mind) and that upsets you. You know: Because ... stupid reasons!
				modifier = opinion_ungrateful 
				who = event_target:is_rape_victim
			}
		}
		narrative_event = { id = DWT.3308 } 			# Back to step 1 as we proceed as initially planned, but this time more violent (poor thing!)
	}
}

					who = event_target:is_rape_victim
				}			
			}
			clr_character_flag = raping_prisoner
			death = { death_reason = death_murder_butchered } 
		}
		# Done!
	}
}

# .3308 Violent Male ruler decides to rape male prisoner and chooses what to do with him. Same as 3000, but more violently pictures and text, because now we're pissed and on a power trip.

	desc = DWT.3308.desc
	
	picture = DWTMaleGayEmbraceBehind
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {

			limit = {

						has_character_flag = victim_lost_brawl

					}
				}
			}
			#If there is, we then grab victim for the event
			location = {
				random_province_character = {
					limit = {
						has_character_flag = victim_lost_brawl
						ai = yes
					}
					save_event_target_as = is_rape_victim
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	trigger = {
		event_target:is_rape_victim = { character = yes } # 
			
	}

# Anal rape of male through male liege - act #2
narrative_event = { 
	id = DWT.3321
	desc = DWT.3321.desc
	picture = DWTMaleGaysAssfuck

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { 
		trigger = {
			event_target:is_rape_victim = { character = yes } # 
			
		}
		name = DWToptionGayMaleComes
		event_target:is_rape_victim = {
			add_trait = raped		# mark the victim as raped
			remove_trait = proud
			add_trait = depressed
			opinion = {								# She will hate you
				modifier = opinion_raped_me
				who = event_target:is_rapist
			}
			if = {
				limit = { trait = strong } 
				random = {
					chance = 15
					remove_trait = strong
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { trait = weak }
				random = {
					chance = 10
					add_trait = ill
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { trait = strong } }
				random = {
					chance = 5
					remove_trait = strong
				}
			}
			opinion = {								# He will hate you more in the next few days with the rape fresh on his mind
				modifier = raper_ruler
				who = event_target:is_rapist
			}
		}
		event_target:is_rapist = { 					# calling the character event, you're the scope
			add_trait = rapist
			if = {
				limit = { 							# if you are a recognised virgin we remove this trait:
					trait = virgin 
				}
				remove_trait = virgin
			}
		}
		narrative_event = { id = DWT.3323 }
	}
}

				modifier = dw_opinion_asshole
				who = event_target:is_rapist
			}
			add_character_modifier = { name = dwt_rape_trauma duration = 30 }
			clr_character_flag = victim_lost_brawl
			clr_character_flag = rape_target
			# Check if rapist is asocial:
			if = {
				limit = {
					event_target:is_rapist = {
						trait = asocial
					}
				}
				health = -2.5
				opinion = {
					modifier = opinion_raped_me2
					who = event_target:is_rapist
				}
			}
		}
		event_target:is_rapist = { 					# calling the character event, you're the scope
			opinion = {								# Oh, you had your fun with her!
				modifier = dw_opinion_good_fuck
				who = event_target:is_rape_victim
			}
			clr_character_flag = raping_prisoner
		}
		narrative_event = { id = DWT.3340 }	# Done - end of chain, check if she dies
	}
}

		event_target:is_rape_victim = { character = yes }
		event_target:is_rape_victim = { NOT = { health = 0.1 } }
	}
	
	option = { 
		trigger = {
			event_target:is_rape_victim = { character = yes }
			#event_target:is_rape_victim = { NOT = { health = 0.1 } }
		}
		name = DWToptionMaleRapeVictimDies
		event_target:is_rape_victim = { 
			clr_character_flag = victim_lost_brawl
			clr_character_flag = rape_target
			death = { death_reason = dwt_death_rape_prisoner } 
			any_dynasty_member = {
				limit = { NOT = { character = event_target:is_rape_victim } }
				opinion = {
					modifier = opinion_killed_close_kin
					who = event_target:is_rapist
				}
				prestige = -5
				piety = -1
			}
			father = { 
				opinion = {
					modifier = opinion_executed_child
					who = event_target:is_rapist
				}
			}
			mother = { 
				opinion = {
					modifier = opinion_executed_child
					who = event_target:is_rapist
				}
			}
			spouse = { 
				opinion = {
					modifier = opinion_spouse_slayer
					who = event_target:is_rapist
				}
			}
			any_child = {
				opinion = {
					modifier = opinion_killed_close_kin
					who = event_target:is_rapist
				}			
			}
		}
		event_target:is_rapist = { 					# calling the character event, you're the scope
			clr_character_flag = raping_prisoner
		}
		# Done!
	}
}

# The victim is brave, strong, shrewd or lunatic enough to fight back - fight #1:

		name = DWTRapeMaleFleesFightHim

				chance = 15

			}

			opinion = {								# Funny, isn't it?

# The victim is brave, strong, shrewd or lunatic enough to fight back - fight - you win or loose #2:
narrative_event = { 
	id = DWT.3403
	hide_window = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		event_target:is_rape_victim = { character = yes }
	}

	# Determine how the fight goes:
	immediate = {
		random_list = {		
			25 = { #80%
				# Rapist wins and proceeds with violent rape:
				# For this we mark the victim as having lost the brawl:
				event_target:is_rape_victim = { set_character_flag = victim_lost_brawl }
				narrative_event = { id = DWT.3404 }
			} 
			25 = { #9%
				# Rapist wins, but victim dies:
				narrative_event = { id = DWT.3405 }
			} 
			25 = { #10%
				# Victim wins and flees:
				narrative_event = { id = DWT.3406 }
			} 
			25 = { #1%
				# Victim wins and rapist dies:
				narrative_event = { id = DWT.3407 }
			}

# Victim lost fight and we continue with what we had in mind:
narrative_event = { 
	id = DWT.3404
	desc = DWT.3404.desc
	picture = DWTMFFight5

	is_triggered_only = yes

	# When we get here we lost the scope and need to reacquire it again. That's why we set flags:
	immediate = {
		if = { # Grab Victim if available:
			limit = {
				location = {
					any_province_character = {
						has_character_flag = victim_lost_brawl
						ai = yes
					}
				}
			}
			# If there is, we then grab the Victim for the event
			location = {
				random_province_character = {
					limit = {
						has_character_flag = victim_lost_brawl
						ai = yes
					}
					save_event_target_as = is_rape_victim
				}
			}
		}
		if = { # Grab Rapist if available:
			limit = {
				location = {
					any_province_character = {
						has_character_flag = raping_prisoner
						ai = no
					}
				}
			}
			# If there is, we then grab the Rapist for the event
			location = {
				random_province_character = {
					limit = {
						has_character_flag = raping_prisoner
						ai = no
					}
					save_event_target_as = is_rapist
				}
			}
		}
	}
		
	option = { 
		trigger = {
			has_character_flag = victim_lost_brawl
			event_target:is_rape_victim = { character = yes } # 
		}
		name = DWToptionNowYouReMine
		event_target:is_rape_victim = {
			remove_trait = honest
			add_trait = deceitful
			opinion = {								# He will hate you for a looooong time.
				modifier = immortal_hate
				who = event_target:is_rapist
			}
		}
		event_target:is_rapist = { 					# calling the character event, you're the scope
			opinion = {								# He refused your 'gift' (you only had her 'best' in mind) and that upsets you. You know: Because ... stupid reasons!
				modifier = opinion_ungrateful 
				who = event_target:is_rape_victim
			}
		}
		narrative_event = { id = DWT.3408 } 		# Back to step 1 as we proceed as initially planned, but this time more violent (poor thing!)
	}
}

narrative_event = {
	id = DWT.3408
	desc = DWT.3408.desc
	
	picture = DWTMFFight5

			limit = {

					}

					limit = {

						ai = yes
					}
					save_event_target_as = is_rape_victim
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	trigger = {
		event_target:is_rape_victim = { character = yes } # 
	}

#### The acts:
# Vaginal rape of male through female liege - act #1
narrative_event = { 
	id = DWT.3410
	desc = DWT.3410.desc
	picture = BleachCowGirlInsertion

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { 
		trigger = {
			event_target:is_rape_victim = { character = yes } # 
		}
		name = DWToptionfurther
		event_target:is_rape_victim = {
			if = {
				limit = { 			# if victim is a recognised virgin, you ruin his virginhood, and he will hate you even more
					trait = virgin 
				}
				remove_trait = virgin
				prestige = -5
				piety = -10
				opinion = {
					modifier = opinion_took_virginity_by_force
					who = event_target:is_rapist
				}
				any_dynasty_member = {
					limit = { NOT = { dynasty = event_target:is_rape_victim } }
					opinion = {
						modifier = opinion_took_family_members_virginity_by_force
						who = event_target:is_rapist
					}
					prestige = -5
					piety = -10
				}
				spouse = { 
					opinion = {
						modifier = opinion_took_family_members_virginity_by_force
						who = event_target:is_rapist
					}
					prestige = -5
					piety = -10
				}
				event_target:is_rapist = {
					prestige = 15
					piety = -10
				}
			}
			add_trait = raped		# mark the victim as raped
		}
		event_target:is_rapist = { 	# calling the character event, you're the scope
			add_trait = rapist
			random = {
				chance = 25			
				add_trait = proud
			}
			if = {
				limit = { 			# if you are a recognised virgin we remove this trait:
					trait = virgin 
				}
				remove_trait = virgin
			}
		}
		narrative_event = { id = DWT.3411 }
	}
}

# Vaginal rape of male through female liege - act #3
narrative_event = { 
	id =  DWT.3412
	desc = DWT.3412.desc
	picture = BleachCowGirlRiding2

	is_triggered_only = yes

	# Creampie:
	option = { 
		trigger = {
			event_target:is_rape_victim = { character = yes } # 
		}
		name = DWTRapeGetCreampie
		event_target:is_rape_victim = {
			if = {
				limit = { trait = strong } 
				random = {
					chance = 15
					remove_trait = strong
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { trait = weak }
				random = {
					chance = 10
					add_trait = ill
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { trait = strong } }
				random = {
					chance = 5
					remove_trait = strong
				}
			}
			opinion = {								# Because we're a mysogonist we assume that he liked it, too.
				modifier = dw_opinion_good_fuck
				who = event_target:is_rapist
			}
			add_character_modifier = { name = dw_good_sex duration = 30 }
			opinion = {								# He will hate you more in the next few days with the rape fresh on her mind
				modifier = raper_ruler
				who = event_target:is_rapist
			}
		}
		event_target:is_rapist = { 					# calling the character event, you're the scope
			if = {
				limit = { trait = weak } 
				random = {
					chance = 25
					remove_trait = weak
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { trait = strong } }
				random = {
					chance = 15
					add_trait = strong
					remove_trait = weak
				}
			}
			if = { 
				limit = {							# if you are under 40 and not pregnant, 25% chance to get pregnant
					NOT = { practical_age = 40 }
					is_pregnant = no
					fertility = 0.5
				}
				random = { 
					chance = 25
					impregnate = event_target:is_rape_victim
				}
			}
		}
		narrative_event = { id = DWT.3413 }
	}
	# Pull out:
	option = { 
		trigger = {
			event_target:is_rape_victim = { character = yes }
		}
		name = DWTRapeGetNoCreampie
		event_target:is_rape_victim = {
			remove_trait = strong
			opinion = {								# He will hate you more in the next few days with the rape fresh on her mind
				modifier = raper_ruler
				who = event_target:is_rapist
			}
		}
		event_target:is_rapist = { 					# calling the character event, you're the scope
			if = {
				limit = { trait = weak } 
				random = {
					chance = 25
					remove_trait = weak
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { trait = strong } }
				random = {
					chance = 15
					add_trait = strong
					remove_trait = weak
				}
			}
			opinion = {								# Oh, you had your fun with him!
				modifier = dw_opinion_good_fuck
				who = event_target:is_rape_victim
			}
			add_character_modifier = { name = dw_good_sex duration = 30 }
		}
		narrative_event = { id = DWT.3414 }
	}
}
