# Victim lost too much health during the rape and dies:
narrative_event = { 
	id = DWT.3440
	desc = DWT.3440.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_DWTr004

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		event_target:is_rape_victim = { character = yes }
		event_target:is_rape_victim = { NOT = { health = 0.1 } }
	}
	
	option = { 
		trigger = {
			event_target:is_rape_victim = { character = yes }
			#event_target:is_rape_victim = { NOT = { health = 0.1 } }
		}
		name = DWToptionRapeVictimDies
		event_target:is_rape_victim = { 
			clr_character_flag = victim_lost_brawl
			clr_character_flag = rape_target
			death = { death_reason = dwt_death_rape_prisoner } 
			any_dynasty_member = {
				limit = { NOT = { character = event_target:is_rape_victim } }
				opinion = {
					modifier = opinion_killed_close_kin
					who = event_target:is_rapist
				}
				prestige = -5
				piety = -1
			}
			father = { 
				opinion = {
					modifier = opinion_executed_child
					who = event_target:is_rapist
				}
			}
			mother = { 
				opinion = {
					modifier = opinion_executed_child
					who = event_target:is_rapist
				}
			}
			spouse = { 
				opinion = {
					modifier = opinion_spouse_slayer
					who = event_target:is_rapist
				}
			}
			any_child = {
				opinion = {
					modifier = opinion_killed_close_kin
					who = event_target:is_rapist
				}			
			}
		}
		event_target:is_rapist = { 					# calling the character event, you're the scope
			clr_character_flag = raping_prisoner
		}
		# Done!
	}
}

# Vaginal sex with willing male courtier and female liege - act #1
narrative_event = { 
	id = DWT.3510
	desc = DWT.3510.desc
	picture = BleachVagPenfromBehind

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { 
		trigger = {
			event_target:is_lustful_participant = { character = yes } # 
		}
		name = DWToptionfurther
		event_target:is_lustful_participant = {
			if = {
				limit = { 						# if victim is a recognised virgin and you take his virginity, then he will be forever grateful
					trait = virgin 
				}
				remove_trait = virgin
				prestige = -1
				piety = -3
				opinion = {
					modifier = opinion_took_virginity
					who = event_target:is_rapist
				}
				spouse = { 
					opinion = {
						modifier = opinion_took_family_members_virginity_by_force		# Because this is the spouse. So it must have been rape in their eyes, right?
						who = event_target:is_rapist
					}
					prestige = -5
					piety = -10
				}
				event_target:is_rapist = {
					prestige = 15
					piety = -10
				}
			}
		}
		event_target:is_rapist = { 	# calling the character event, you're the scope
			if = {
				limit = { 			# if you are a recognised virgin we remove this trait:
					trait = virgin 
				}
				opinion = {
					modifier = opinion_took_virginity								# You will forever remember that he was your first!
					who = event_target:is_lustful_participant
				}
				remove_trait = virgin
			}
		}
		narrative_event = { id = DWT.3511 }
	}
}

# Vaginal sex with willing male courtier and female liege - act #3
narrative_event = { 
	id =  DWT.3512
	desc = DWT.3512.desc
	picture = BleachVagPenFromBelow

	is_triggered_only = yes

	# Creampie:
	option = { 
		trigger = {
			event_target:is_lustful_participant = { character = yes } # 
		}
		name = DWTRapeGetCreampie
		event_target:is_lustful_participant = {
			opinion = {								# Because we're a mysogonist we assume that he liked it, too.
				modifier = dw_opinion_good_fuck
				who = event_target:is_rapist
			}
			add_character_modifier = { name = dw_good_sex duration = 30 }
			if = { 
				limit = {							# if victim under 40 and not pregnant, 25% chance to get pregnant
					NOT = { practical_age = 40 }
					is_pregnant = no
					fertility = 0.5
				}
				random = { 
					chance = 25
					impregnate = event_target:is_rapist
				}
			}
		}
		event_target:is_rapist = { 					# calling the character event, you're the scope
			if = {
				limit = { trait = weak } 
				random = {
					chance = 10
					remove_trait = weak
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { trait = strong } }
				random = {
					chance = 5
					add_trait = strong
					remove_trait = weak
				}
			}
		}
		narrative_event = { id = DWT.3513 }
	}
	# Pull out:
	option = { 
		trigger = {
			event_target:is_lustful_participant = { character = yes } # 
		}
		name = DWTRapeGetNoCreampie
		event_target:is_lustful_participant = {
			opinion = {								# Because we're a mysogonist we assume that he liked it, too.
				modifier = dw_opinion_good_fuck
				who = event_target:is_rapist
			}
		}
		event_target:is_rapist = { 					# calling the character event, you're the scope
			if = {
				limit = { trait = weak } 
				random = {
					chance = 10
					remove_trait = weak
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { trait = strong } }
				random = {
					chance = 5
					add_trait = strong
					remove_trait = weak
				}
			}
			opinion = {								# Oh, you had your fun with her!
				modifier = dw_opinion_good_fuck
				who = event_target:is_lustful_participant
			}
			add_character_modifier = { name = dw_good_sex duration = 30 }
		}
		narrative_event = { id = DWT.3514 }
	}
}

		}

		event_target:is_lustful_participant = {
			opinion = {								# Because we're a mysogonist we assume that he liked it, too.
				modifier = dw_opinion_good_fuck
				who = event_target:is_rapist
			}
		}
		event_target:is_rapist = { 	# calling the character event, you're the scope
			if = {
				limit = { 			# if you are a recognised virgin we remove this trait:
					trait = virgin 
				}
				remove_trait = virgin
			}
		}

				}

				random = {
					chance = 5
					remove_trait = strong

				who = event_target:is_rapist

			if = {
				limit = { trait = weak } 
				random = {
					chance = 25
					remove_trait = weak

					remove_trait = weak

			}

					# And he might turn into a slut/lover:

					remove_trait = celibate
					remove_trait = depressed
					add_trait = lustful
					add_trait = ambitious
					add_lover = event_target:is_rapist
				}
			}
		}

		event_target:is_lustful_participant = {
			opinion = {								# Because we're a mysogonist we assume that he liked it, too.
				modifier = dw_opinion_good_fuck
				who = event_target:is_rapist
			}
			clr_character_flag = victim_lost_brawl
			clr_character_flag = rape_target
		}
		event_target:is_rapist = { 					# calling the character event, you're the scope
			opinion = {								# Oh, you had your fun with her!
				modifier = dw_opinion_good_fuck
				who = event_target:is_lustful_participant
			}
			clr_character_flag = raping_courtier
		}
	}
}

			prisoner = no
			in_command = yes
			
		}

		location = {
				any_province_character = {

					AND = {						
						#is_female = yes
						is_adult = yes
						#NOT = { practical_age = 30 }
						#trait = virgin
						ai = yes
					}
			}
		}
	}
	immediate = {

	if = { #chasing women

					AND = {
						is_female = no

		}

# You won a siege, we have suitable 'targets' and therefore we show the pop-up:
narrative_event = {	
	id = DWT.8000
	desc = DWT.8000.desc
	picture = DTWSackingOfRome
	
	is_triggered_only = yes		# triggered from on_action: on_siege_won_leader{}

	trigger = { 
		in_command = yes
		prisoner = no
		OR = {
			is_female = no
			trait = futa
		}
			
		OR = {
			trait = cambion
			trait = alu_fiend
			trait = incubus
			trait = lilith
			trait = rapist
			trait = cruel
			trait = viking
			trait = ravager
			trait = pirate
			trait = seaking
			trait = sea_queen
		}
			
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1

		modifier = {
			factor = 50
			FROM = { spouse = { is_ruler = yes } }
			OR = { FROM = { father = { is_ruler = yes } } }
			OR = { FROM = { mother = { is_ruler = yes } } }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 24
			trait = virgin
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 10
			NOT = { practical_age = 20 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 4
			trait = bombshell
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 3
			trait = fair
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = lustful
		}
	}	
	
	immediate = {
		# Find priority target:
		if = { 
			limit = {
				location = {
					any_province_character = {
						is_female = yes
						practical_age = 16
						NOT = { practical_age = 30 }
						ai = yes
					}
				}
			}
			#If there is, we then grab one for the event
			location = {
				any_province_character = {
					limit = {
						is_female = yes
						practical_age = 16
						NOT = { practical_age = 30 }
						ai = yes
					}
					save_event_target_as = is_booty_primary
				}
			}
		}
		# Find second choice:
		if = { 
			limit = {
				NOT = { character = event_target:is_booty_primary }
				location = {
					any_province_character = {
						is_female = yes
						practical_age = 16
						NOT = { practical_age = 30 }
						ai = yes
					}
				}
			}
			#If there is, we then grab one for the event
			location = {
				any_province_character = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { character = event_target:is_booty_primary }
						is_female = yes
						practical_age = 16
						NOT = { practical_age = 30 }
						ai = yes
					}
					save_event_target_as = is_zweite_wahl
				}
			}
		}
		# Find a third choice:
		if = { 
			limit = {
				NOT = { character = event_target:is_booty_primary }
				NOT = { character = event_target:is_zweite_wahl }
				location = {
					any_province_character = {
						is_female = yes
						practical_age = 16
						NOT = { practical_age = 45 }
						ai = yes
					}
				}
			}
			#If there is, we then grab one for the event
			location = {
				any_province_character = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { character = event_target:is_booty_primary }
						NOT = { character = event_target:is_zweite_wahl }
						is_female = yes
						practical_age = 16
						NOT = { practical_age = 45 }
						ai = yes
					}
					save_event_target_as = is_dritte_wahl
				}
			}
		}
		ROOT = {
			save_event_target_as = is_rapist
			set_character_flag = raping_courtier
		}
	}

	option = { 												# Do we have booty?
		trigger = {
			event_target:is_booty_primary = { character = yes }
		}
		name = DWT.8000.optBS
		event_target:is_booty_primary = {
			opinion = {
				modifier = dw_opinion_intimidated
				who = ROOT
				months = 3
			}
			set_character_flag = rape_target
			save_event_target_as = is_rape_victim
			clr_character_flag = siege_victor_recent
		}
		narrative_event = { id = DWT.8001 }
	}	
	option = { 												# Do we have booty?
		trigger = {
			event_target:is_zweite_wahl = { character = yes }
		}
		name = DWT.8000.optFair
		event_target:is_zweite_wahl = {
			opinion = {
				modifier = dw_opinion_intimidated
				who = ROOT
				months = 3
			}
			set_character_flag = rape_target
			save_event_target_as = is_rape_victim
			clr_character_flag = siege_victor_recent
		}
		narrative_event = { id = DWT.8001 }
	}	
	option = { 												# Do we have booty?
		trigger = {
			event_target:is_dritte_wahl = { character = yes }
		}
		name = DWT.8000.resteficken
		event_target:is_dritte_wahl = {
			opinion = {
				modifier = dw_opinion_intimidated
				who = ROOT
				months = 3
			}
			set_character_flag = rape_target
			save_event_target_as = is_rape_victim
			clr_character_flag = siege_victor_recent
		}
		narrative_event = { id = DWT.8001 }
	}
	option = {												# Hags!
		name = DWT.8000.optNeg
		clr_character_flag = siege_victor_recent
	}

}

narrative_event = {
	id = DWT.8001
	desc = "DWT.8001.desc"
	picture = DTWBootySelection
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		clr_character_flag = siege_victor_recent
		if = { 												# Grab victim if available:
			limit = {
				location = {
					any_province_character = {
						has_character_flag = rape_target
						ai = yes
					}
				}
			}
			#If there is, we then grab one for the event
			location = {
				random_province_character = {
					limit = {
						has_character_flag = rape_target
						ai = yes
					}
					save_event_target_as = is_rape_victim
				}
			}
		}
		if = { 												# Grab victim if available:
			limit = {
				location = {
					any_province_character = {
						has_character_flag = raping_courtier
						ai = no
					}
				}
			}
			#If there is, we then grab one for the event
			location = {
				random_province_character = {
					limit = {
						has_character_flag = raping_courtier
						ai = no
					}
					save_event_target_as = is_rapist
				}
			}
		}
	}
	# Vaginal rape decission:
	option = { 
		trigger = {
			event_target:is_rape_victim = { character = yes }
		}
		name = DWT.8001.vaginal
		event_target:is_rape_victim = {
			prestige = -15
			piety = -5
			# Piss off their entire dynasty, too:
			if = {
				limit = { 
					event_target:is_rape_victim = { 
						NOT = { dynasty = event_target:is_rapist } 
					}
				}
				liege = {									# Piss off their liege (a little):
					opinion = {
						modifier = opinion_raped_subject
						who = event_target:is_rapist
					}
					prestige = -1
					piety = -2
				}
				any_dynasty_member = {
					limit = { NOT = { character = event_target:is_rape_victim } }
					opinion = {
						modifier = opinion_raped_family
						who = event_target:is_rapist
					}
					prestige = -5
					piety = -3
				}
				spouse = { 
					opinion = {
						modifier = opinion_raped_spouse
						who = event_target:is_rapist
					}
				}
				prestige = -15
				piety = -5
				clr_character_flag  = victim_lost_brawl # As we start fresh, victim should *not* (yet) have this flag anyway.
				imprison = event_target:is_rapist
			}			
		}
		event_target:is_rapist = { 					# calling the character event, you're the scope
			prestige = 5
			piety = -15
		}
		narrative_event = { id = DWT.8010 } 
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { 
		trigger = {
			event_target:is_rape_victim = { character = yes } # 
		}
		name = DWToptionfurther
		event_target:is_rape_victim = {
			if = {
				limit = { 			# if victim is a recognised virgin, you ruin her virginhood, and she will hate you even more
					trait = virgin 
				}
				remove_trait = virgin
				prestige = -5
				piety = -10
				opinion = {
					modifier = opinion_took_virginity_by_force
					who = event_target:is_rapist
				}
				any_dynasty_member = {
					limit = { NOT = { dynasty = event_target:is_rape_victim } }
					opinion = {
						modifier = opinion_took_family_members_virginity_by_force
						who = event_target:is_rapist
					}
					prestige = -5
					piety = -10
				}
				spouse = { 
					opinion = {
						modifier = opinion_took_family_members_virginity_by_force
						who = event_target:is_rapist
					}
					prestige = -5
					piety = -10
				}
				event_target:is_rapist = {
					prestige = 15
					piety = -10
				}
			}
			add_trait = raped		# mark the victim as raped
		}
		event_target:is_rapist = { 	# calling the character event, you're the scope
			add_trait = rapist
			
			if = {
				limit = { 			# if you are a recognised virgin we remove this trait:
					trait = virgin 
				}
				remove_trait = virgin
			}
		}
		narrative_event = { id = DWT.8011 }
	}
}

		}

		picture = 210_3
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	# Creampie:
	option = { 
		trigger = {
			event_target:is_rape_victim = { character = yes } # 
		}
		name = DWTRapeDoCreampie
		event_target:is_rape_victim = {
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { trait = strong } }
				random = {
					chance = 20
					add_trait = abdominal_pain
				}
				random = {
					chance = 20
					add_trait = cramps
				}
				random = {
					chance = 20
					add_trait = rash
				}
				random = {
					chance = 20
					add_trait = infection
				}
			}

			if = {
				limit = { trait = strong  }
				random = {
					chance = 10
					add_trait = abdominal_pain
				}
				random = {
					chance = 10
					add_trait = cramps
				}
				random = {
					chance = 10
					add_trait = rash
				}
				random = {
					chance = 10
					add_trait = infection
				}
			}
			opinion = {								# She will hate you more in the next few days with the rape fresh on her mind
				modifier = raper_ruler
				who = event_target:is_rapist
			}
			if = { 
				limit = {							# if victim under 40 and not pregnant, 25% chance to get pregnant
					NOT = { practical_age = 40 }
					is_pregnant = no
					fertility = 0.5
				}
				random = { 
					chance = 25
					impregnate = event_target:is_rapist
				}
			}
		}
		event_target:is_rapist = { 					# calling the character event, you're the scope
			if = {
				limit = { trait = chaste } 
				random = {
					chance = 75
					remove_trait = weak
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { trait = lustful } }
				random = {
					chance = 25
					add_trait = lustful
					remove_trait = chaste
				}
			}
		}
		narrative_event = { id = DWT.8013 }
	}
	# Pull out:
	option = { 
		trigger = {
			event_target:is_rape_victim = { character = yes } # 
		}
		name = DWTRapeNoCreampie
		event_target:is_rape_victim = {
			opinion = {								# She will hate you more in the next few days with the rape fresh on her mind
				modifier = raper_ruler
				who = event_target:is_rapist
			}
		}
		event_target:is_rapist = { 					# calling the character event, you're the scope
			if = {
				limit = { trait = chaste } 
				random = {
					chance = 75
					remove_trait = weak
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { trait = lustful } }
				random = {
					chance = 25
					add_trait = lustful
					remove_trait = chaste
				}
			}
			
			opinion = {								# Oh, you had your fun with her!
				modifier = dw_opinion_good_fuck
				who = event_target:is_rape_victim
			}
			add_character_modifier = { name = dw_good_sex duration = 30 }
		}
		narrative_event = { id = DWT.8014 }
	}
}

	option = { 
		trigger = {
			event_target:is_rape_victim = { character = yes } # 
		}
		name = DWTDoneWithVaginalRape
		event_target:is_rape_victim = {
			opinion = {								# She will be disgusted that you came in her
				modifier = dw_opinion_asshole
				who = event_target:is_rapist
			}
			add_character_modifier = { name = dwt_rape_trauma duration = 30 }
			clr_character_flag = victim_lost_brawl
			clr_character_flag = rape_target
			# Check if rapist is asocial:
			if = {
				limit = {
					event_target:is_rapist = {
						trait = asocial
					}
				}
				health = -2.5
				opinion = {
					modifier = opinion_raped_me2
					who = event_target:is_rapist
				}
			}
		}
		event_target:is_rapist = { 					# calling the character event, you're the scope
			opinion = {								# Oh, you had your fun with her!
				modifier = dw_opinion_good_fuck
				who = event_target:is_rape_victim
			}
			add_character_modifier = { name = dw_good_sex duration = 30 }
			clr_character_flag = raping_prisoner
		}
		narrative_event = { id = DWT.8040 }	# Done - end of chain, check if she dies
	}
}

    }

	# And we're done. Aren't we?
	option = { 
		trigger = {
			event_target:is_rape_victim = { character = yes } # 
		}
		name = DWTDoneNoCreampie
		event_target:is_rape_victim = {
			opinion = {								# Either way she will be disgusted
				modifier = dw_opinion_asshole
				who = event_target:is_rapist
			}
			add_character_modifier = { name = dwt_rape_trauma duration = 30 }
			clr_character_flag = victim_lost_brawl
			clr_character_flag = rape_target
		}
		event_target:is_rapist = { 					# calling the character event, you're the scope
			opinion = {								# Oh, you had your fun with her!
				modifier = dw_opinion_good_fuck
				who = event_target:is_rape_victim
			}
			clr_character_flag = raping_prisoner
		}
		narrative_event = { id = DWT.8040 }	# Done - end of chain, check if she dies
	}
}

	option = { 
		trigger = {
			event_target:is_rape_victim = { character = yes } # 
		}
		name = DWToptionfurther
		event_target:is_rape_victim = {
			opinion = {
				modifier = dw_opinion_sexual_disgust
				who = event_target:is_rapist
			}
			add_trait = raped		# mark the victim as raped
		}
		event_target:is_rapist = { 	# calling the character event, you're the scope
			add_trait = rapist
			random = {
				chance = 25			
				add_trait = proud
			}
			if = {
				limit = { 			# if you are a recognised virgin we remove this trait:
					trait = virgin 
				}
				remove_trait = virgin
			}
		}
		narrative_event = { id = DWT.8021 }
	}
}

	option = { 
		trigger = {
			event_target:is_rape_victim = { character = yes } # 
		}
		name = DWT.8022.option
		event_target:is_rape_victim = {
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { trait = strong } }
				random = {
					chance = 25
					add_trait = abdominal_pain
				}
				random = {
					chance = 25
					add_trait = cramps
				}
				random = {
					chance = 25
					add_trait = diarrhea
				}
				random = {
					chance = 25
					add_trait = infection
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { trait = strong  }
				random = {
					chance = 15
					add_trait = abdominal_pain
				}
				random = {
					chance = 15
					add_trait = cramps
				}
				random = {
					chance = 10
					add_trait = diarrhea
				}
				random = {
					chance = 10
					add_trait = infection
				}
			}
			opinion = {								# Because we're a mysogonist we assume that she liked it, too.
				modifier = dw_opinion_good_fuck
				who = event_target:is_rapist
			}
			opinion = {								# She will hate you more in the next few days with the rape fresh on her mind
				modifier = raper_ruler
				who = event_target:is_rapist
			}
			# Check if rapist is asocial:
			if = {
				limit = {
					event_target:is_rapist = {
						trait = asocial
					}
				}
				health = -2.5
				opinion = {
					modifier = opinion_raped_me2
					who = event_target:is_rapist
				}
			}
		}
		event_target:is_rapist = { 					# calling the character event, you're the scope
			if = {
				limit = { trait = chaste } 
				random = {
					chance = 75
					remove_trait = weak
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { trait = lustful } }
				random = {
					chance = 25
					add_trait = lustful
					remove_trait = chaste
				}
			}
		}
		narrative_event = { id = DWT.8023 }
	}
}

	# Let her swallow:
	option = { 
		trigger = {
			event_target:is_rape_victim = { character = yes } # 
		}
		name = DWT.8032.option
		event_target:is_rape_victim = {
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { trait = strong } }
				random = {
					chance = 20
					add_trait = chest_pain
				}
				random = {
					chance = 20
					add_trait = cough
				}
				random = {
					chance = 10
					add_trait = headache
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { trait = strong  }
				random = {
					chance = 10
					add_trait = chest_pain
				}
				random = {
					chance = 10
					add_trait = cough
				}
				random = {
					chance = 5
					add_trait = headache
				}
			}
			opinion = {								# She will hate you 
				modifier = raper_ruler
				who = event_target:is_rapist
			}
			# Check if rapist is asocial:
			if = {
				limit = {
					event_target:is_rapist = {
						trait = asocial
					}
				}
				health = -2.5
				opinion = {
					modifier = opinion_raped_me2
					who = event_target:is_rapist
				}
			}
		}
		narrative_event = { id = DWT.8033 }
	}
}

# Victim lost too much health during the rape and dies:
narrative_event = { 
	id = DWT.8040
	desc = DWT.8040.desc
	picture = DWTRapeBadEnd

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		event_target:is_rape_victim = { character = yes }
		event_target:is_rape_victim = { NOT = { health = 0.1 } }
	}
	
	option = { 
		trigger = {
			event_target:is_rape_victim = { character = yes }
			#event_target:is_rape_victim = { NOT = { health = 0.1 } }
		}
		name = DWToptionRapeVictimDies
		event_target:is_rape_victim = { 
			clr_character_flag = victim_lost_brawl
			clr_character_flag = rape_target
			death = { death_reason = dwt_death_rape_prisoner } 
			any_dynasty_member = {
				limit = { NOT = { character = event_target:is_rape_victim } }
				opinion = {
					modifier = opinion_killed_close_kin
					who = event_target:is_rapist
				}
				prestige = -5
				piety = -1
			}
			father = { 
				opinion = {
					modifier = opinion_executed_child
					who = event_target:is_rapist
				}
			}
			mother = { 
				opinion = {
					modifier = opinion_executed_child
					who = event_target:is_rapist
				}
			}
			spouse = { 
				opinion = {
					modifier = opinion_spouse_slayer
					who = event_target:is_rapist
				}
			}
			any_child = {
				opinion = {
					modifier = opinion_killed_close_kin
					who = event_target:is_rapist
				}			
			}
		}
		event_target:is_rapist = { 					# calling the character event, you're the scope
			clr_character_flag = raping_prisoner
		}
		# Done!
	}
}

##siege victory chain for male target preference
# You won a siege, we have suitable 'targets' and therefore we show the pop-up:
narrative_event = {	
	id = DWT.8050
	desc = DWT.8000.desc
	picture = DTWSackingOfRome
	
	is_triggered_only = yes		# triggered from on_action: on_siege_won_leader{}

	trigger = { 
		siege = {
			is_attacker = yes
		}
		in_command = yes
		prisoner = no
		OR = {
									trait = cambion
									trait = alu_fiend
			trait = incubus
			trait = lilith
			trait = cruel
			trait = viking
			trait = rapist
		}
			
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1

		modifier = {
			factor = 50
			FROM = { spouse = { is_ruler = yes } }
			OR = { FROM = { father = { is_ruler = yes } } }
			OR = { FROM = { mother = { is_ruler = yes } } }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 24
			trait = virgin
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 10
			NOT = { practical_age = 20 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 4
			trait = robust
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 4
			trait = strong
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 3
			trait = fair
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = lustful
		}
	}	
	
	immediate = {
		# Find priority target:
		if = { 
			limit = {
				location = {
					any_province_character = {
						is_female = no
						practical_age = 16
						NOT = { practical_age = 30 }
						ai = yes
					}
				}
			}
			#If there is, we then grab one for the event
			location = {
				any_province_character = {
					limit = {
						is_female = no
						practical_age = 16
						NOT = { practical_age = 30 }
						ai = yes
					}
					save_event_target_as = is_booty_primary
				}
			}
		}
		# Find second choice:
		if = { 
			limit = {
				NOT = { character = event_target:is_booty_primary }
				location = {
					any_province_character = {
						is_female = no
						practical_age = 16
						NOT = { practical_age = 30 }
						ai = yes
					}
				}
			}
			#If there is, we then grab one for the event
			location = {
				any_province_character = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { character = event_target:is_booty_primary }
						is_female = no
						practical_age = 16
						NOT = { practical_age = 30 }
						ai = yes
					}
					save_event_target_as = is_zweite_wahl
				}
			}
		}
		# Find a third choice:
		if = { 
			limit = {
				NOT = { character = event_target:is_booty_primary }
				NOT = { character = event_target:is_zweite_wahl }
				location = {
					any_province_character = {
						is_female = no
						practical_age = 16
						NOT = { practical_age = 45 }
						ai = yes
					}
				}
			}
			#If there is, we then grab one for the event
			location = {
				any_province_character = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { character = event_target:is_booty_primary }
						NOT = { character = event_target:is_zweite_wahl }
						is_female = no
						practical_age = 16
						NOT = { practical_age = 45 }
						ai = yes
					}
					save_event_target_as = is_dritte_wahl
				}
			}
		}
		ROOT = {
			save_event_target_as = is_rapist
			set_character_flag = raping_courtier
		}
	}

	option = { 												# Do we have booty?
		trigger = {
			event_target:is_booty_primary = { character = yes }
		}
		name = DWT.8050.optBS
		event_target:is_booty_primary = {
			opinion = {
				modifier = dw_opinion_intimidated
				who = ROOT
				months = 3
			}
			set_character_flag = rape_target
			save_event_target_as = is_rape_victim
			clr_character_flag = siege_victor_recent
		}
		narrative_event = { id = DWT.8001 }
	}	
	option = { 												# Do we have booty?
		trigger = {
			event_target:is_zweite_wahl = { character = yes }
		}
		name = DWT.8050.optFair
		event_target:is_zweite_wahl = {
			opinion = {
				modifier = dw_opinion_intimidated
				who = ROOT
				months = 3
			}
			set_character_flag = rape_target
			save_event_target_as = is_rape_victim
			clr_character_flag = siege_victor_recent
		}
		narrative_event = { id = DWT.8001 }
	}	
	option = { 												# Do we have booty?
		trigger = {
			event_target:is_dritte_wahl = { character = yes }
		}
		name = DWT.8050.resteficken
		event_target:is_dritte_wahl = {
			opinion = {
				modifier = dw_opinion_intimidated
				who = ROOT
				months = 3
			}
			set_character_flag = rape_target
			save_event_target_as = is_rape_victim
			clr_character_flag = siege_victor_recent
		}
		narrative_event = { id = DWT.8001 }
	}
	option = {												# Worthless!
		name = DWT.8050.optNeg
		clr_character_flag = siege_victor_recent
	}

}


narrative_event = {
	id = DWT.8051
	desc = "DWT.8051.desc"
	picture = DTWBootySelection
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		clr_character_flag = siege_victor_recent
		if = { 												# Grab victim if available:
			limit = {
				location = {
					any_province_character = {
						has_character_flag = rape_target
						ai = yes
					}
				}
			}
			#If there is, we then grab one for the event
			location = {
				random_province_character = {
					limit = {
						has_character_flag = rape_target
						ai = yes
					}
					save_event_target_as = is_rape_victim
				}
			}
		}
		if = { 												# Grab victim if available:
			limit = {
				location = {
					any_province_character = {
						has_character_flag = raping_courtier
						ai = no
					}
				}
			}
			#If there is, we then grab one for the event
			location = {
				random_province_character = {
					limit = {
						has_character_flag = raping_courtier
						ai = no
					}
					save_event_target_as = is_rapist
				}
			}
		}
	}
	# Vaginal rape decission:
	option = { 
		trigger = {
			ROOT = { is_female = yes } #not really valid for men
			event_target:is_rape_victim = { character = yes }
		}
		name = DWT.8051.vaginal
		event_target:is_rape_victim = {
			prestige = -15
			piety = -5
			# Piss off their entire dynasty, too:
			if = {
				limit = { 
					event_target:is_rape_victim = { 
						NOT = { dynasty = event_target:is_rapist } 
					}
				}
				liege = {									# Piss off their liege (a little):
					opinion = {
						modifier = opinion_raped_subject
						who = event_target:is_rapist
					}
					prestige = -1
					piety = -2
				}
				any_dynasty_member = {
					limit = { NOT = { character = event_target:is_rape_victim } }
					opinion = {
						modifier = opinion_raped_family
						who = event_target:is_rapist
					}
					prestige = -5
					piety = -3
				}
				spouse = { 
					opinion = {
						modifier = opinion_raped_spouse
						who = event_target:is_rapist
					}
				}
				prestige = -15
				piety = -5
				clr_character_flag  = victim_lost_brawl # As we start fresh, victim should *not* (yet) have this flag anyway.
				imprison = event_target:is_rapist
			}			
		}
		event_target:is_rapist = { 					# calling the character event, you're the scope
			prestige = 5
			piety = -15
		}
		narrative_event = { id = DWT.8010 } 
	}
	# Anal rape decission:
	option = {

			event_target:is_rape_victim = { character = yes } #

#
### We marked an enemy general as 'enemy_leader' and now fire on that event.
#

# You lost a battle you were leading as female liege. We check if we have suitable 'targets' before we do the pop-up:
narrative_event = {
	id = DWT.8100
	
	ai = no
	
	desc = DWT.8100.desc
	picture = DWTLeonidas	
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = { 
		is_alive = yes
		is_female = yes
		trait = lilith
		FROM = { 
			any_army = {
				center_flank_leader = {
					is_female = no
					save_event_target_as = enemy_leader
					set_character_flag = enemy_leader
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	# ROOT: You (female liege in command)
	# FROM: Opposing general

	immediate = {
		ROOT = { 
			save_event_target_as = is_rape_victim
		}
		FROM = { 
			any_army = {
				center_flank_leader = {
					is_female = no
					save_event_target_as = enemy_leader
					set_character_flag = enemy_leader
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = DWT.8100.option
		ROOT = {
			opinion = {								
				modifier = opinion_rape_fight
				who = event_target:enemy_leader
			}
			prestige = 5
			piety = -1
		}
		event_target:enemy_leader = {
			prestige = 15
			piety = -10
			opinion = {								
				modifier = dw_opinion_good_brawl
				who = ROOT
			}
			prestige = -15
			piety = -10
		}

		narrative_event = { id = DWT.8101 }
	}
}

# The act:
narrative_event = {	
	id = DWT.8101
	desc = DWT.8101.desc
	picture = TroopFemaleLiegeAmbush3
	
	is_triggered_only = yes



	immediate = {
		if = { 	# Grab enemy leader if available:
			limit = {
				location = {
					any_province_character = {
						has_character_flag = enemy_leader
						ai = yes
					}
				}
			}
			#If there is, we then grab one for the event
			location = {
				random_province_character = {
					limit = {
						has_character_flag = enemy_leader
						ai = yes
					}
					save_event_target_as = enemy_leader
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		trigger = {
			event_target:enemy_leader = { character = yes } # 
		}
		name = DWT.8101.option
		ROOT = {
			opinion = {
				modifier = dw_rape_trauma 
				who = event_target:enemy_leader
			}
			add_trait = raped						# mark the victim as raped
			hidden_tooltip = {
				add_character_modifier = { name = dwt_rape_trauma duration = 30 }
				opinion = {
					modifier = opinion_raped_me
					who = event_target:enemy_leader
				}
			}
			prestige = -15
			piety = -10
			if = {
				limit = { 							# if agressor is a recognised virgin, you ruin her virginhood, and she will hate you even more
					trait = virgin 
				}
				remove_trait = virgin
				prestige = -15
				piety = -10
				opinion = {
					modifier = opinion_took_virginity_by_force
					who = event_target:enemy_leader
				}
				hidden_tooltip = {
					any_dynasty_member = {
						limit = { NOT = { dynasty = event_target:enemy_leader } }
						opinion = {
							modifier = opinion_took_family_members_virginity_by_force
							who = event_target:enemy_leader
						}
						prestige = -5
						piety = -10
					}
					spouse = { 
						opinion = {
							modifier = opinion_took_family_members_virginity_by_force
							who = event_target:enemy_leader
						}
						prestige = -5
						piety = -10
					}
				}
			}
			if = { 
				limit = {							# if victim under 40 and not pregnant, 25% chance to get pregnant
					NOT = { practical_age = 40 }
					is_pregnant = no
					#fertility = 0.5
				}
				character_event = { id = DWT.9000 }
			}
		}
		event_target:enemy_leader = {
			opinion = {
				modifier = dw_opinion_good_fuck
				who = ROOT
			}
			hidden_tooltip = {
				add_character_modifier = { name = dw_good_sex duration = 30 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { 							# if agressor is a recognised virgin, then he looses it and remebers you fondly as his first
					trait = virgin 
				}
				remove_trait = virgin
				prestige = 15
				piety = 10
				opinion = {
					modifier = opinion_took_virginity
					who = ROOT
				}
			}
			prestige = 15
			piety = -10
			add_trait = rapist
			clr_character_flag = enemy_leader
		}
	}
}

# You lost a battle you were leading as female liege. We check if we have suitable 'targets' before we do the pop-up:
narrative_event = {
	id = DWT.8200
	
	ai = no
	
	desc = DWT.8100.desc
	picture = DTWSackingOfRome	
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
			has_rape_content = yes
		}	
	hide_window = yes 						# nothing to see here
	
	# ROOT: You (female liege in command)
	# FROM: Opposing general

	immediate = {
		ROOT = { 
			save_event_target_as = is_looser
			
		}
		FROM = { 
			any_army = {
				center_flank_leader = {
					is_female = no
					save_event_target_as = enemy_leader
					set_character_flag = enemy_leader
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	if = {
		limit = {
			event_target:enemy_leader = { character = yes } # 
		}
		#name = DWT.8100.option
		#log = "DWT.8100: [Root.GetTitledName] becomes victim of [From.GetTitledName]"
		narrative_event = { id = DWT.8100 }
	}
}

	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

		#ROOT = { save_event_target_as = new_dad }

	}

# .9010 Female event to see if they got pregnant from a non-existent person (commoner)(ROOT = female)
character_event = {
	id = DWT.9010
	
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		if = { # If pregnant we terminate the pregnancy check in order to avoid a double pregnancy.
			limit = {
				is_pregnant = yes
			}
			ROOT = { remove_virginity_trait = yes } # Check to remove Virgin trait
			break = yes 
		}		
		if = { # If the woman isn't married, then we handle it as a simple impregnate
			limit = {
				is_married = no
			}
			random = {
				chance = 1
				modifier = {
					factor = 10
					ROOT = { fertility = 0.25 }
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 2
					ROOT = { fertility = 0.5 }
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 2
					ROOT = { fertility = 0.75 }
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.5
					ROOT = { fertility = 1 }
				}
				ROOT = { impregnate = yes } # Woman is knocked by the unknown
			}
			ROOT = { remove_virginity_trait = yes } # Check to remove Virgin trait
			break = yes
		}
		if = { # If the woman is married, but the male is not her husband, then we process this as an impregnate_cuckoo.
			limit = {
				is_married = yes
			}
			random = {
				chance = 1
				modifier = {
					factor = 10
					ROOT = { fertility = 0.25 }
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 2
					ROOT = { fertility = 0.5 }
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 2
					ROOT = { fertility = 0.75 }
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.5
					ROOT = { fertility = 1 }
				}
				ROOT = { impregnate_cuckoo = yes } # Woman is knocked by the unknown
			}
			ROOT = { remove_virginity_trait = yes } # Check to remove Virgin trait
			break = yes
		}
	}
}
